{AvŚat, 1}
buddho bhagavān satkṛto gurukṛto mānitaḥ pūjito rājabhī rājamātrair dhanibhiḥ pauraiḥ śreṣṭhibhiḥ sārthavāhair devair nāgair yakṣair asurair garuḍaiḥ kinnarair mahoragair iti devanāgayakṣāsuragaruḍakinnaramahoragābhyarcito buddho bhagavān jñāto mahāpuṇyo lābhī cīvarapiṇḍapātaśayanāsanaglānapratyayabhaiṣajyapariṣkārāṇāṃ saśrāvakasaṃgho rājagṛham upaniśritya viharati veṇuvane kalandakanivāpe | [AvŚat, 1 1.1]
tatra bhagavato 'cirābhisaṃbuddhabodher yaśasā ca sarvaloka āpūrṇaḥ | [AvŚat, 1 1.2]
atha dakṣiṇāgiriṣu janapade saṃpūrṇo nāma brāhmaṇamahāśālaḥ prativasati āḍhyo mahādhano mahābhogo vistīrṇaviśālaparigraho vaiśravaṇadhanasamudito vaiśravaṇadhanapratispardhī | [AvŚat, 1 2.1]
sa ca śrāddho bhadraḥ kalyāṇāśaya ātmahitaparahitapratipannaḥ kāruṇiko mahātmā dharmakāmaḥ prajāvatsalas tyāgaruciḥ pradānaruciḥ pradānābhirato mahati tyāge vartate | [AvŚat, 1 2.2]
yāvad asau sarvapāṣaṇḍikaṃ yajñam ārabdho yaṣṭum yatrānekāni tīrthikaśatasahasrāṇi bhuñjate sma | [AvŚat, 1 3.1]
yadā bhagavatā rājā bimbisāraḥ saparivāro vinītaḥ tasya ca vinayād bahūni prāṇiśatasahasrāṇi vinayam upagatāni tadā rājagṛhāt pūrṇasya jñātayo 'bhyāgatya pūrṇasya purastād buddhasya varṇaṃ bhāṣayituṃ pravṛttā dharmasya saṃghasya ca | [AvŚat, 1 3.2]
atha pūrṇo brāhmaṇamahāśālo bhagavato guṇasaṃkīrtanaṃ pratiśrutya mahāntaṃ prasādaṃ pratilabdhavān | [AvŚat, 1 3.3]
tataḥ śaraṇam abhiruhya rājagṛhābhimukhaḥ sthitvā ubhau jānumaṇḍale pṛthivyāṃ pratiṣṭhāpya puṣpāṇi kṣipan dhūpam udakaṃ ca bhagavantam āyācituṃ pravṛttaḥ āgacchatu bhagavān yajñaṃ me anubhavituṃ yajñavāṭam iti | [AvŚat, 1 3.4]
atha tāni puṣpāṇi buddhānāṃ buddhānubhāvena devatānāṃ ca devatānubhāvenopari bhagavataḥ puṣpamaṇḍapaṃ kṣiptvā tasthuḥ dhūpo 'bhrakūṭavad udakaṃ vaiḍūryaśalākavat | [AvŚat, 1 3.5]
athāyuṣmān ānandaḥ kṛtakarapuṭo bhagavantaṃ papraccha kuta idaṃ bhadanta nimantraṇam āyātam iti | [AvŚat, 1 4.1]
bhagavān āha dakṣiṇāgiriṣv ānanda janapade saṃpūrṇo nāma brāhmaṇamahāśālaḥ prativasati tatrāsmābhir gantavyam sajjībhavantu bhikṣava iti | [AvŚat, 1 4.2]
bhagavān bhikṣusahasraparivṛtto dakṣiṇāgiriṣu janapade cārikāṃ caritvā pūrṇasya brāhmaṇamahāśālasya yajñavāṭasamīpe sthitvā cintām āpede yannvahaṃ pūrṇabrāhmaṇam ṛddhiprātihāryeṇāvarjayeyam iti | [AvŚat, 1 4.3]
atha bhagavāṃs taṃ bhikṣusahasram antardhāpya ekaḥ pātracarakavyagrahastaḥ pūrṇasamīpe sthitaḥ | [AvŚat, 1 4.4]
atha pūrṇo brāhmaṇamahāśālo bhagavantaṃ dadarśa dvātriṃśatā mahāpuruṣalakṣaṇaiḥ samalaṃkṛtam aśītyā cānuvyañjanair virājitagātraṃ vyāmaprabhālaṃkṛtaṃ sūryasahasrātirekaprabhaṃ jaṅgamam iva ratnaparvataṃ samantato bhadrakam | [AvŚat, 1 4.5]
dṛṣṭvā ca punas tvaritatvaritaṃ bhagavataḥ samīpam upasaṃkramya bhagavantam uvāca svāgataṃ bhagavan niṣīdatu bhagavān kriyatāṃ āsanaparigraho mamānugrahārtham iti | [AvŚat, 1 4.6]
bhagavān āha yadi te parityaktaṃ dīyatām asmin pātra iti | [AvŚat, 1 4.7]
atha pūrṇo brāhmaṇamahāśālaḥ pañcamāṇavakaśataparivṛto bhagavato vividhabhakṣyabhojyakhādyalehyapeyacoṣyādibhir āhārair ārabdhaḥ pātraṃ paripūrayitum | [AvŚat, 1 4.8]
bhagavān api svakāt pātrād bhikṣupātreṣv āhāraṃ saṃkramayati | [AvŚat, 1 4.9]
yadā bhagavato viditaṃ pūrṇāni bhikṣusahasrasya pātrāṇīti tadā svapātraṃ pūrṇam ādarśitam | [AvŚat, 1 4.10]
tato bhikṣusahasraṃ pūrṇapātram ardhacandrākāreṇa darśitavān | [AvŚat, 1 4.11]
devatābhir apy ākāśasthābhiḥ śabdam udīritam pūrṇāni bhagavato bhikṣusahasrasya ca pātrāṇīti | [AvŚat, 1 4.12]
tataḥ prātihāryadarśanāt pūrṇaḥ prasādajāto mūlanikṛtta iva drumo hṛṣṭatuṣṭapramuditaḥ udagraprītisaumanasyajāto bhagavataḥ pādayor nipatya praṇidhiṃ kartum ārabdhaḥ anenāhaṃ kuśalamūlena cittotpādena deyadharmaparityāgena ca andhe loke anāyake apariṇāyake buddho bhūyāsam atīrṇānāṃ sattvānāṃ tārayitā amuktānāṃ mocayitā anāśvastānām āśvāsayitā aparinirvṛtānāṃ parinirvāpayiteti | [AvŚat, 1 4.13]
atha bhagavān pūrṇasya brāhmaṇamahāśālasya hetuparaṃparāṃ karmaparaṃparāṃ ca jñātvā smitaṃ prāvirakārṣīt | [AvŚat, 1 5.1]
dharmatā khalu yasmin samaye buddhā bhagavantaḥ smitaṃ prāviṣkurvanti tasmin samaye nīlapītalohitāvadātā arciṣo mukhān niścārya kāścid adhastād gacchanti kāścid upariṣṭād gacchanti | [AvŚat, 1 5.2]
yā adhastād gacchanti tāḥ saṃjīvaṃ kālasūtraṃ saṃghātaṃ rauravaṃ mahārauravaṃ tapanaṃ pratāpanam avīcim arbudaṃ nirarbudaṃ aṭaṭaṃ hahavaṃ huhuvam utpalaṃ padmaṃ mahāpadmaṃ narakān gatvā ye uṣṇanarakās teṣu śītībhūtā nipatanti ye śītanarakās teṣu uṣṇībhūtā nipatanti | [AvŚat, 1 5.3]
tena teṣāṃ sattvānāṃ kāraṇāviśeṣāḥ pratiprasrabhyante | [AvŚat, 1 5.4]
teṣām evaṃ bhavati kiṃ nu vayaṃ bhavanta itaś cyutāḥ āhosvid anyatropapannā iti | [AvŚat, 1 5.5]
teṣāṃ prasādasaṃjananārthaṃ bhagavān nirmitaṃ visarjayati | [AvŚat, 1 5.6]
teṣāṃ nirmitaṃ dṛṣṭvaivaṃ bhavati na hyeva vayaṃ bhavantaḥ itaś cyutāḥ nāpy anyatropapannāḥ api tv ayam apūrvadarśanaḥ sattvaḥ asyānubhāvenāsmākaṃ kāraṇāviśeṣāḥ pratiprasrabdhā iti | [AvŚat, 1 5.7]
te nirmite cittam abhiprasādya tan narakavedanīyaṃ karma kṣapayitvā devamanuṣyeṣu pratisandhiṃ gṛhṇanti yatra satyānāṃ bhājanabhūtā bhavanti | [AvŚat, 1 5.8]
yā upariṣṭād gacchanti tāś cāturmahārājikāṃs trayastriṃśān yāmāṃs tuṣitān nirmāṇaratīn paranirmitavaśavartino brahmakāyikān brahmapurohitān mahābrahmaṇaḥ parīttābhān apramāṇābhān ābhāsvarān parīttaśubhān apramāṇaśubhāñ śubhakṛtsnān anabhrakān puṇyaprasavān bṛhatphalān abṛhān atapān sudṛśān sudarśanān akaniṣṭhān devān gatvā anityaṃ duḥkhaṃ śūnyam anātmety udghoṣayanti gāthādvayaṃ ca bhāṣante | [AvŚat, 1 5.9]
ārabhadhvaṃ niṣkrāmata yujyadhvaṃ buddhaśāsane | [AvŚat, 1 5.10]
dhunīta mṛtyunaḥ sainyaṃ naḍāgāram iva kuñjaraḥ | [AvŚat, 1 5.11]
yo hy asmin dharmavinaye apramattaś cariṣyati | [AvŚat, 1 6.1]
prahāya jātisaṃsāraṃ duḥkhasyāntaṃ kariṣyati | [AvŚat, 1 6.2]
atha tā arciṣas trisāhasramahāsāhasraṃ lokadhātum anvāhiṇḍya bhagavantam eva pṛṣṭhataḥ pṛṣṭhataḥ samanugacchanti | [AvŚat, 1 7.1]
tad yadi bhagavān atītaṃ karma vyākartukāmo bhavati bhagavataḥ pṛṣṭhato 'ntardhīyante | [AvŚat, 1 7.2]
anāgataṃ vyākartukāmo bhavati purastād antardhīyante | [AvŚat, 1 7.3]
narakopapattiṃ vyākartukāmo bhavati pādatale 'ntardhīyante | [AvŚat, 1 7.4]
tiryagupapattiṃ vyākartukāmo bhavati pārṣṇyām antardhīyante | [AvŚat, 1 7.5]
pretopapattiṃ vyākartukāmo bhavati pādāṅguṣṭhe 'ntardhīyante | [AvŚat, 1 7.6]
manuṣyopapattiṃ vyākartukāmo bhavati jānunor antardhīyante | [AvŚat, 1 7.7]
balacakravartirājyaṃ vyākartukāmo bhavati vāme karatale 'ntardhīyante | [AvŚat, 1 7.8]
cakravartirājyaṃ vyākartukāmo bhavati dakṣiṇe karatale 'ntardhīyante | [AvŚat, 1 7.9]
devopapattiṃ vyākartukāmo bhavati nābhyām antardhīyante | [AvŚat, 1 7.10]
śrāvakabodhiṃ vyākartukāmo bhavati āsye 'ntardhīyante | [AvŚat, 1 7.11]
pratyekabodhiṃ vyākartukāmo bhavati ūrṇāyām antardhīyante | [AvŚat, 1 7.12]
anuttarāṃ samyaksaṃbodhiṃ vyākartukāmo bhavati uṣṇīṣe antardhīyante | [AvŚat, 1 7.13]
atha tā arciṣo bhagavantaṃ triḥ pradakṣiṇīkṛtya bhagavata uṣṇīṣe 'ntarhitāḥ | [AvŚat, 1 8.1]
athāyuṣmān ānandaḥ kṛtakarapuṭo bhagavantaṃ papraccha | [AvŚat, 1 8.2]
nānāvidho raṅgasahasracitro vaktrāntarān niṣkasitaḥ kalāpaḥ | [AvŚat, 1 8.3]
avabhāsitā yena diśaḥ samantād divākareṇodayatā yathaiva | [AvŚat, 1 8.4]
gāthāḥ ca bhāṣate | [AvŚat, 1 628004_1]
vigatodbhavā dainyamadaprahīṇā buddhā jagaty uttamahetubhūtāḥ | [AvŚat, 1 9.2]
nākāraṇaṃ śaṅkhamṛṇālagauraṃ smitam upadarśayanti jinā jitārayaḥ | [AvŚat, 1 9.3]
tatkālaṃ svayam adhigamya vīra buddhyā śrotṝṇāṃ śramaṇa jinendra kāṅkṣitānām | [AvŚat, 1 10.1]
dhīrābhir munivṛṣa vāgbhir uttamābhir utpannaṃ vyapanaya saṃśayaṃ śubhābhiḥ | [AvŚat, 1 10.2]
nākasmāllavaṇajalādrirājadhairyāḥ saṃbuddhāḥ smitam upadarśayanti nāthāḥ | [AvŚat, 1 11.1]
yasya arthe smitam upadarśayanti dhīrāḥ tam śrotum samabhilaṣanti te jana oghāḥ | [AvŚat, 1 628010_1]
bhagavān āha evam etad ānanda evam etat | [AvŚat, 1 12.1]
nāhetvapratyayam ānanda tathāgatā arhantaḥ samyaksaṃbuddhāḥ smitaṃ prāviṣkurvanti | [AvŚat, 1 12.2]
eṣa ānanda pūrṇo brāhmaṇamahāśālaḥ | [AvŚat, 1 12.3]
anena kuśalamūlena cittotpādena deyadharmaparityāgena ca trikalpāsaṃkhyeyasamudānītāṃ bodhiṃ samudānīya mahākaruṇāparibhāvitāḥ ṣaṭ pāramitāḥ paripūrya pūrṇabhadro nāma samyaksaṃbuddho bhaviṣyati daśabhir balaiś caturbhir vaiśāradyais tribhir āveṇikaiḥ smṛtyupasthānair mahākaruṇayā ca | [AvŚat, 1 12.4]
ayam asya deyadharmo yo mamāntike cittaprasāda iti | [AvŚat, 1 12.5]
bhūyas ca anena citrāṇi kuśala mūlāni samavaropitāni | [AvŚat, 1 628016_1]
tasmāt tarhi bhikṣava evaṃ śikṣitavyaṃ yacchāstāraṃ satkariṣyāmo gurukariṣyāmo mānayiṣyāmaḥ pūjayiṣyāmaḥ śāstāraṃ satkṛtya gurukṛtya mānayitvā pūjayitvopaniśritya vihariṣyāmaḥ | [AvŚat, 1 14.1]
ity evaṃ vo bhikṣavaḥ śikṣitavyam | [AvŚat, 1 14.2]
idam avocat bhagavān | [AvŚat, 1 628019_1]
ātta manasaḥ te bhikṣavaḥ bhagavataḥ bhāṣitam abhyanandan | [AvŚat, 1 628020_1]
{AvŚat, 2}
buddho bhagavān satkṛto gurukṛto mānitaḥ pūjito rājabhī rājamātrair dhanibhiḥ pauraiḥ śreṣṭhibhiḥ sārthavāhair devair nāgair yakṣair asurair garuḍaiḥ kinnarair mahoragair iti devanāgayakṣāsuragaruḍakinnaramahoragābhyarcito buddho bhagavān jñāto mahāpuṇyo lābhī cīvarapiṇḍapātaśayanāsanaglānapratyayabhaiṣajyapariṣkārāṇāṃ saśrāvakasaṃgho vaiśālīm upaniśritya viharati markaṭahradatīre kūṭāgāraśālāyām | [AvŚat, 2 1.1]
atha pūrvāhṇe nivāsya pātracīvaram ādāya bhikṣugaṇaparivṛto bhikṣusaṃghapuraskṛto vaiśālīṃ piṇḍāya prāvikṣat | [AvŚat, 2 1.2]
sāvadānīṃ vaiśālīṃ piṇḍāya caritvā yena siṃhasya senāpater niveśanaṃ tenopasaṃkrāntaḥ | [AvŚat, 2 1.3]
upasaṃkramya prajñapta evāsane niṣaṇṇaḥ | [AvŚat, 2 1.4]
atha siṃhasya senāpateḥ snuṣā yaśomatī nāma abhirūpā darśanīyā prāsādikā | [AvŚat, 2 2.1]
sā bhagavato vicitralakṣaṇojjvalakāyaṃ dṛṣṭvā atyarthaṃ prasādaṃ labdhavatī | [AvŚat, 2 2.2]
sā śvaśuraṃ papraccha asti kaścid upāyo yenāham apy evaṃguṇayuktā syām iti | [AvŚat, 2 2.3]
atha siṃhasya senāpater etad abhavat udārādhimuktā bateyaṃ dārikā | [AvŚat, 2 2.4]
yadi punar iyaṃ pratyayam āsādayet kuryād anuttarāyāṃ samyaksaṃbodhau praṇidhānam iti viditvoktavān dārike yadi hetuṃ samādāya vartiṣyasi tvam apy evaṃvidhā bhaviṣyasi yādṛśo bhagavān iti | [AvŚat, 2 2.5]
tataḥ siṃhena senāpatinā yaśomatyāḥ prasādābhivṛddhyarthaṃ prabhūtaṃ hiraṇyasuvarṇaṃ ratnāni ca dattāni | [AvŚat, 2 3.1]
tato yaśomatyā dārikayā bhagavān saśrāvakasaṃghaḥ śvo 'ntargṛhe bhaktenopanimantritaḥ | [AvŚat, 2 3.2]
adhivāsitaṃ ca bhagavatā tasyā anugrahārtham | [AvŚat, 2 3.3]
atha yaśomatī dārikā suvarṇamayāni puṣpāṇi kārayitvā rūpyamayāṇi ratnamayāni prabhūtagandhamālyavilepanasaṃgrahaṃ kṛtvā śatarasam āhāraṃ sajjīkṛtya bhagavato dūtena kālam ārocayati samayo bhadanta sajjaṃ bhaktaṃ yasyedānīṃ bhagavān kālaṃ manyata iti | [AvŚat, 2 4.1]
atha bhagavān bhikṣugaṇaparivṛto bhikṣusaṃghapuraskṛto yena siṃhasya senāpater niveśanaṃ tenopasaṃkrāntaḥ | [AvŚat, 2 4.2]
upasaṃkramya purastād bhikṣusaṃghasya prajñapta evāsane niṣaṇṇaḥ | [AvŚat, 2 4.3]
atha yaśomatī dārikā sukhopaniṣaṇṇaṃ buddhapramukhaṃ bhikṣusaṃghaṃ viditvā śatarasenāhāreṇa svahastaṃ saṃtarpya puṣpāṇi bhagavati kṣeptum ārabdhā | [AvŚat, 2 4.4]
atha tāni puṣpāṇi upari bhagavato ratnakūṭāgāro ratnacchatraṃ ratnamaṇḍapa ivāvasthitam yanna śakyaṃ suśikṣitena karmakāreṇa karmāntevāsinā vā kartum yathāpi tad buddhānāṃ buddhānubhāvena devatānāṃ ca devānubhāvena | [AvŚat, 2 4.5]
atha yaśomatī dārikā tad atyadbhutaṃ devamanuṣyāvarjanakaraṃ prātihāryaṃ dṛṣṭvā mūlanikṛtta iva drumaḥ sarvaśarīreṇa bhagavataḥ pādayor nipatya praṇidhānaṃ kartum ārabdhā anenāhaṃ kuśalamūlena cittotpādena deyadharmaparityāgena ca andhe loke anāyake apariṇāyake buddho bhūyāsam atīrṇānāṃ sattvānāṃ tārayitā amuktānāṃ mocayitā anāśvastānām āśvāsayitā aparinirvṛtānāṃ parinirvāpayiteti | [AvŚat, 2 5.1]
atha bhagavān yaśomatyā dārikāyā hetuparaṃparāṃ karmaparaṃparāṃ ca jñātvā smitaṃ prāvirakārṣīt | [AvŚat, 2 6.1]
dharmatā khalu yasmin samaye buddhā bhagavantaḥ smitaṃ prāviṣkurvanti tasmin samaye nīlapītalohitāvadātā arciṣo mukhān niścārya kāścid adhastād gacchanti kāścid upariṣṭād gacchanti | [AvŚat, 2 6.2]
yā adhastād gacchanti tāḥ saṃjīvaṃ kālasūtraṃ saṃghātaṃ rauravaṃ mahārauravaṃ tapanaṃ pratāpanam avīcim arbudaṃ nirarbudaṃ aṭaṭaṃ hahavaṃ huhuvam utpalaṃ padmaṃ mahāpadmaṃ narakān gatvā ye uṣṇanarakāsteṣu śītībhūtā nipatanti ye śītanarakās teṣu uṣṇībhūtā nipatanti | [AvŚat, 2 6.3]
tena teṣāṃ sattvānāṃ kāraṇāviśeṣāḥ pratiprasrabhyante | [AvŚat, 2 6.4]
teṣām evaṃ bhavati kiṃ nu vayaṃ bhavanta itaś cyutāḥ āhosvid anyatropapannā iti | [AvŚat, 2 6.5]
teṣāṃ prasādasaṃjananārthaṃ bhagavān nirmitaṃ visarjayati | [AvŚat, 2 6.6]
teṣāṃ nirmitaṃ dṛṣṭvaivaṃ bhavati na hy eva vayaṃ bhavantaḥ itaś cyutāḥ nāpy anyatropapannāḥ api tv ayam apūrvadarśanaḥ sattvaḥ asyānubhāvenāsmākaṃ kāraṇāviśeṣāḥ pratiprasrabdhā iti | [AvŚat, 2 6.7]
te nirmite cittam abhiprasādya tan narakavedanīyaṃ karma kṣapayitvā devamanuṣyeṣu pratisandhiṃ gṛhṇanti yatra satyānāṃ bhājanabhūtā bhavanti | [AvŚat, 2 6.8]
yā upariṣṭād gacchanti tāś cāturmahārājikāṃs trayastriṃśān yāmāṃs tuṣitān nirmāṇaratīn paranirmitavaśavartino brahmakāyikān brahmapurohitān mahābrahmaṇaḥ parīttābhān apramāṇābhān ābhāsvarān parīttaśubhān apramāṇaśubhāñ śubhakṛtsnān anabhrakān puṇyaprasavān bṛhatphalān abṛhān atapān sudṛśān sudarśanān akaniṣṭhān devān gatvā anityaṃ duḥkhaṃ śūnyam anātmety udghoṣayanti gāthādvayaṃ ca bhāṣante | [AvŚat, 2 6.9]
ārabhadhvaṃ niṣkrāmata yujyadhvaṃ buddhaśāsane | [AvŚat, 2 6.10]
dhunīta mṛtyunaḥ sainyaṃ naḍāgāram iva kuñjaraḥ | [AvŚat, 2 6.11]
yo hy asmin dharmavinaye apramattaś cariṣyati | [AvŚat, 2 7.1]
prahāya jātisaṃsāraṃ duḥkhasyāntaṃ kariṣyati | [AvŚat, 2 7.2]
iti | [AvŚat, 2 7.3]
atha tā arciṣas trisāhasramahāsāhasraṃ lokadhātum anvāhiṇḍya bhagavantam eva pṛṣṭhataḥ pṛṣṭhataḥ samanugacchanti | [AvŚat, 2 8.1]
tad yadi bhagavān atītaṃ karma vyākartukāmo bhavati bhagavataḥ pṛṣṭhato 'ntardhīyante | [AvŚat, 2 8.2]
anāgataṃ vyākartukāmo bhavati purastād antardhīyante | [AvŚat, 2 8.3]
narakopapattiṃ vyākartukāmo bhavati pādatale 'ntardhīyante | [AvŚat, 2 8.4]
tiryagupapattiṃ vyākartukāmo bhavati pārṣṇyām antardhīyante | [AvŚat, 2 8.5]
pretopapattiṃ vyākartukāmo bhavati pādāṅguṣṭhe 'ntardhīyante | [AvŚat, 2 8.6]
manuṣyopapattiṃ vyākartukāmo bhavati jānunor antardhīyante | [AvŚat, 2 8.7]
balacakravartirājyaṃ vyākartukāmo bhavati vāme karatale 'ntardhīyante | [AvŚat, 2 8.8]
cakravartirājyaṃ vyākartukāmo bhavati dakṣiṇe karatale 'ntardhīyante | [AvŚat, 2 8.9]
devopapattiṃ vyākartukāmo bhavati nābhyām antardhīyante | [AvŚat, 2 8.10]
śrāvakabodhiṃ vyākartukāmo bhavati āsye 'ntardhīyante | [AvŚat, 2 8.11]
pratyekabodhiṃ vyākartukāmo bhavati ūrṇāyām antardhīyante | [AvŚat, 2 8.12]
anuttarāṃ samyaksaṃbodhiṃ vyākartukāmo bhavati uṣṇīṣe antardhīyante | [AvŚat, 2 8.13]
atha tā arciṣo bhagavantaṃ triḥ pradakṣiṇīkṛtya bhagavata uṣṇīṣe 'ntarhitāḥ | [AvŚat, 2 9.1]
athāyuṣmān ānandaḥ kṛtakarapuṭo bhagavantaṃ papraccha | [AvŚat, 2 9.2]
nānāvidho raṅgasahasracitro vaktrāntarān niṣkasitaḥ kalāpaḥ | [AvŚat, 2 9.3]
avabhāsitā yena diśaḥ samantād divākareṇodayatā yathaiva | [AvŚat, 2 9.4]
gāthāś ca bhāṣate | [AvŚat, 2 10.1]
vigatodbhavā dainyamadaprahīṇā buddhā jagaty uttamahetubhūtāḥ | [AvŚat, 2 10.2]
nākāraṇaṃ śaṅkhamṛṇālagauraṃ smitam upadarśayanti jinā jitārayaḥ | [AvŚat, 2 10.3]
tatkālaṃ svayam adhigamya vīra buddhyā śrotṝṇāṃ śramaṇa jinendra kāṅkṣitānām | [AvŚat, 2 11.1]
dhīrābhir munivṛṣa vāgbhir uttamābhir utpannaṃ vyapanaya saṃśayaṃ śubhābhiḥ | [AvŚat, 2 11.2]
nākasmāl lavaṇajalādrirājadhairyāḥ saṃbuddhāḥ smitam upadarśayanti nāthāḥ | [AvŚat, 2 12.1]
yasyārthe smitam upadarśayanti dhīrāḥ taṃ śrotuṃ samabhilaṣanti te janaughāḥ | [AvŚat, 2 12.2]
iti | [AvŚat, 2 12.3]
bhagavān āha evam etad ānanda evam etat | [AvŚat, 2 13.1]
nāhetvapratyayam ānanda tathāgatā arhantaḥ samyaksaṃbuddhāḥ smitaṃ prāviṣkurvanti | [AvŚat, 2 13.2]
paśyasy ānanda anayā yaśomatyā dārikayā mamaivaṃvidhaṃ satkāraṃ kṛtam | [AvŚat, 2 13.3]
evaṃ bhadanta | [AvŚat, 2 13.4]
eṣā ānanda yaśomatī dārikā anena kuśalamūlena cittotpādena deyadharmaparityāgena ca trikalpāsaṃkhyeyasamudānītāṃ bodhiṃ samudānīya mahākaruṇāparibhāvitāḥ ṣaṭ pāramitāḥ paripūrya ratnamatir nāma samyaksaṃbuddho bhaviṣyati daśabhir balaiś caturbhir vaiśāradyais tribhir āveṇikaiḥ smṛtyupasthānair mahākaruṇayā ca | [AvŚat, 2 13.5]
ayam asya deyadharmo yo mamāntike cittasyābhiprasāda iti | [AvŚat, 2 13.6]
idam avocad bhagavān | [AvŚat, 2 14.1]
āttamanasas te bhikṣavo bhagavato bhāṣitam abhyanandan | [AvŚat, 2 14.2]
{AvŚat, 3}
buddho bhagavān satkṛto gurukṛto mānitaḥ pūjito rājabhī rājamātrair dhanibhiḥ pauraiḥ śreṣṭhibhiḥ sārthavāhair devair nāgair yakṣair asurair garuḍaiḥ kinnarair mahoragair iti devanāgayakṣāsuragaruḍakinnaramahoragābhyarcito buddho bhagavān jñāto mahāpuṇyo lābhī cīvarapiṇḍapātaśayanāsanaglānapratyayabhaiṣajyapariṣkārāṇāṃ saśrāvakasaṃghaḥ śrāvastyāṃ viharati jetavane 'nāthapiṇḍadasyārāme | [AvŚat, 3 1.1]
śrāvastyām anyatamaḥ śreṣṭhī prativasati āḍhyo mahādhano mahābhogo vistīrṇaviśālaparigraho vaiśravaṇadhanasamudito vaiśravaṇadhanapratispardhī | [AvŚat, 3 2.1]
tena sadṛśāt kulāt kalatram ānītam | [AvŚat, 3 2.2]
sa tayā sārdhaṃ krīḍati ramate paricārayati | [AvŚat, 3 2.3]
tasya krīḍato ramamāṇasya paricārayato na putro na duhitā | [AvŚat, 3 2.4]
sa kare kapolaṃ dattvā cintāparo vyavasthitaḥ anekadhanasamuditaṃ me gṛham | [AvŚat, 3 2.5]
na me putro na duhitā | [AvŚat, 3 2.6]
mamātyayāt sarvasvāpateyam aputrakam iti kṛtvā rājavidheyaṃ bhaviṣyatīti | [AvŚat, 3 2.7]
sa śramaṇabrāhmaṇanaimittikasuhṛtsaṃbandhibāndhavair ucyate devatāyācanaṃ kuruṣveti | [AvŚat, 3 2.8]
asti caiṣa loke pravādo yadāyācanahetoḥ putrā jāyante duhitaraś ceti | [AvŚat, 3 3.1]
tacca naivam | [AvŚat, 3 3.2]
yady evam abhaviṣyat ekaikasya putrasahasram abhaviṣyat tadyathā rājñaś cakravartinaḥ | [AvŚat, 3 3.3]
api tu trayāṇāṃ sthānānāṃ saṃmukhībhāvāt putrā jāyante duhitaraś ca | [AvŚat, 3 3.4]
katameṣāṃ trayāṇām | [AvŚat, 3 3.5]
mātāpitarau raktau bhavataḥ saṃnipatitau | [AvŚat, 3 3.6]
mātā kalyā bhavati ṛtumatī | [AvŚat, 3 3.7]
gandharvaś ca pratyupasthito bhavati | [AvŚat, 3 3.8]
eṣāṃ trayāṇāṃ sthānānāṃ saṃmukhībhāvāt putrā jāyante duhitaraś ca | [AvŚat, 3 3.9]
tathā hy asau śramaṇabrāhmaṇanaimittikasuhṛtsaṃbandhibāndhavavipralabdho 'putraḥ putrābhinandī śivavaruṇakuberaśakrabrahmādīn anyāṃś ca devatāviśeṣān āyācate sma | [AvŚat, 3 3.10]
tadyathā ārāmadevatā vanadevatāś catvaradevatāḥ śṛṅgāṭakadevatā balipratigrāhikā devatāḥ | [AvŚat, 3 3.11]
sahajāḥ sahadharmikā nityānubandhā api devatā āyācate sma | [AvŚat, 3 3.12]
sa caivam āyācanaparas tiṣṭhati | [AvŚat, 3 3.13]
anyatamaś ca sattvo 'nyatamasmāt sattvanikāyāc cyutvā tasyāḥ prajāpatyāḥ kukṣim avakrāntaḥ | [AvŚat, 3 3.14]
pañcāveṇikā dharmā ekatye paṇḍitajātīye mātṛgrāme | [AvŚat, 3 3.15]
katame pañca | [AvŚat, 3 3.16]
raktaṃ puruṣaṃ jānāti viraktaṃ puruṣaṃ jānāti | [AvŚat, 3 3.17]
kālaṃ jānāti ṛtuṃ jānāti | [AvŚat, 3 3.18]
garbham avakrāntaṃ jānāti | [AvŚat, 3 3.19]
yasya sakāśād garbho 'vakrāmati taṃ jānāti | [AvŚat, 3 3.20]
dārakaṃ jānāti | [AvŚat, 3 3.21]
dārikāṃ jānāti | [AvŚat, 3 3.22]
saced dārako bhavati dakṣiṇaṃ kukṣiṃ niśritya tiṣṭhati | [AvŚat, 3 3.23]
saced dārikā bhavati vāmaṃ kukṣiṃ niśritya tiṣṭhati | [AvŚat, 3 3.24]
sā āttamanāttamanāḥ svāmina ārocayati diṣṭyā āryaputra vardhase | [AvŚat, 3 3.25]
āpannasattvāsmi saṃvṛttā | [AvŚat, 3 3.26]
yathā ca me dakṣiṇaṃ kukṣiṃ niśritya tiṣṭhati niyataṃ dārako bhaviṣyatīti | [AvŚat, 3 3.27]
so 'py āttamanāttamanāḥ pūrvakāyam atyunnamayya dakṣiṇaṃ bāhum abhiprasārya udānam udānayati apy evāhaṃ cirakālābhilaṣitaṃ putramukhaṃ paśyeyam | [AvŚat, 3 3.28]
jāto me syān nāvajātaḥ | [AvŚat, 3 3.29]
kṛtyāni me kurvīta | [AvŚat, 3 3.30]
bhṛtaḥ pratibibhṛyāt | [AvŚat, 3 3.31]
dāyād yaṃ pratipadyeta | [AvŚat, 3 3.32]
kulavaṃśo me cirasthitikaḥ syāt | [AvŚat, 3 3.33]
asmākaṃ cāpy atītakālagatānām alpaṃ vā prabhūtaṃ vā dānāni dattvā kṛtyāni kṛtvā asmākaṃ nāmnā dakṣiṇām ādekṣyati idaṃ tayor yatratatropapannayor gacchator anugacchatviti | [AvŚat, 3 3.34]
āpannasattvāṃ caināṃ viditvopariprāsādatalagatām ayantritāṃ dhārayati | [AvŚat, 3 3.35]
śīte śītopakaraṇair uṣṇe uṣṇopakaraṇair vaidyaprajñaptair āhārair nātitiktair nātyamlair nātilavaṇair nātimadhurair nātikaṭukair nātikaṣāyais tiktāmlalavaṇamadhurakaṭukakaṣāyavivarjitair āhārair hārārdhahāravibhūṣitagātrīm apsarasam iva nandanavanavicāriṇīṃ mañcān mañcaṃ pīṭhāt pīṭham anavatarantīmadharimāṃ bhūmim | [AvŚat, 3 3.36]
na cāsyāḥ kiṃcid amanojñaśabdaśravaṇaṃ yāvad eva garbhasya paripākāya | [AvŚat, 3 3.37]
sā aṣṭānāṃ vā navānāṃ vā māsānām atyayāt prasūtā | [AvŚat, 3 3.38]
dārako jātaḥ | [AvŚat, 3 3.39]
abhirūpo darśanīyaḥ prāsādikaḥ | [AvŚat, 3 3.40]
janmani cāsya tat kulaṃ nanditam | [AvŚat, 3 3.41]
tasya jātau jātimahaṃ kṛtvā nāmadheyaṃ vyavasthāpyate kiṃ bhavatu dārakasya nāmeti | [AvŚat, 3 3.42]
jñātayaḥ ūcuḥ yasmād asya janmani sarvakulaṃ nanditam tasmād bhavatu dārakasya nanda iti nāmeti | [AvŚat, 3 3.43]
tasya nanda iti nāma vyavasthāpitam | [AvŚat, 3 3.44]
so 'ṣṭābhir dhātrībhir unnīyate vardhyate kṣīreṇa dadhnā navanītena sarpiṣā sarpimaṇḍenānyaiś cottaptottaptair upakaraṇaviśeṣaiḥ | [AvŚat, 3 4.1]
āśu vardhate hradastham iva paṅkajam | [AvŚat, 3 4.2]
yadā mahān saṃvṛttaḥ pañcavarṣaḥ ṣaḍvarṣo vā tadā kusīdaḥ saṃvṛttaḥ paramakusīdaḥ | [AvŚat, 3 4.3]
necchati śayanāsanād apy utthātum | [AvŚat, 3 4.4]
tena tīkṣṇaniśitabuddhitayā antargṛhasthenaiva śāstrāṇy adhītāni | [AvŚat, 3 4.5]
atha śreṣṭhina etad abhavat so 'pi me kadācit karhicid devatārādhanayā putro jātaḥ so 'pi kusīdaḥ paramakusīdaḥ | [AvŚat, 3 5.1]
śayanāsanād api nottiṣṭhate | [AvŚat, 3 5.2]
tat kiṃ mamānenedṛgjātīyena putreṇa yo nāma svasthaśarīro bhūtvā paśur iva saṃtiṣṭhatīti | [AvŚat, 3 5.3]
sa ca śreṣṭhī pūraṇābhiprasannaḥ | [AvŚat, 3 6.1]
tena ṣaṭ tīrthikāḥ śāstāraḥ svagṛham āhūtāḥ api nāmāyaṃ dārakas teṣāṃ darśanād gauravajātaḥ śayanāsanād api tāvad uttiṣṭhet | [AvŚat, 3 6.2]
atha kusīdo dārakas tāñśāstṝn dṛṣṭvā cakṣuḥsaṃprekṣaṇām api na kṛtavān kaḥ punar vāda utthāsyati vā abhivādayiṣyati vā āsanena vā upanimantrayiṣyati | [AvŚat, 3 6.3]
atha sa gṛhapatis tām evāvasthāṃ dṛṣṭvā suṣṭhutaram utkaṇṭhitaḥ kare kapolaṃ dattvā cintāparo vyavasthitaḥ | [AvŚat, 3 6.4]
atrāntare nāsti kiṃcid buddhānāṃ bhagavatām ajñātam adṛṣṭam aviditam avijñātam | [AvŚat, 3 6.5]
dharmatā khalu buddhānāṃ bhagavatāṃ mahākāruṇikānāṃ lokānugrahapravṛttakānām ekārakṣāṇāṃ śamathavipaśyanāvihāriṇāṃ tridamathavastukuśalānāṃ caturoghottīrṇānāṃ caturṛddhipādacaraṇatalasupratiṣṭhitānāṃ caturṣu saṃgrahavastuṣu dīrgharātrakṛtaparicayānāṃ pañcāṅgaviprahīṇānāṃ pañcagatisamatikrāntānāṃ ṣaḍaṅgasamanvāgatānāṃ ṣaṭpāramitāparipūrṇānāṃ saptabodhyaṅgakusumāḍhyānām aṣṭāṅgamārgadeśikānāṃ navānupūrvavihārasamāpattikuśalānāṃ daśabalabalināṃ daśadiksamāpūrṇayaśasāṃ daśaśatavaśavartiprativiśiṣṭānāṃ trī rātres trir divasasya ca buddhacakṣuṣā lokaṃ vyavalokya jñānadarśanaṃ pravartate ko hīyate ko vardhate kaḥ kṛcchraprāptaḥ kaḥ saṃkaṭaprāptaḥ kaḥ saṃbādhaprāptaḥ kaḥ kṛcchrasaṃkaṭasaṃbādhaprāptaḥ ko 'pāyanimnaḥ ko 'pāyapravaṇaḥ ko 'pāyaprāgbhāraḥ kam aham apāyād uddhṛtya svarge mokṣe ca pratiṣṭhāpayeyam | [AvŚat, 3 6.6]
kasya kāmapaṅkanimagnasya hastoddhāram anupradadyām | [AvŚat, 3 6.7]
kam āryadhanavirahitam āryadhanaiśvaryādhipatye pratiṣṭhāpayeyam | [AvŚat, 3 6.8]
kasyājñānatimirapaṭalaparyavanaddhanetrasya jñānāñjanaśalākayā cakṣur viśodhayāmi | [AvŚat, 3 6.9]
kasyānavaropitāni kuśalamūlānyavaropayeyam | [AvŚat, 3 6.10]
kasyāvaropitāni paripācayeyam | [AvŚat, 3 6.11]
kasya paripakvāni vimocayeyam | [AvŚat, 3 6.12]
āha ca | [AvŚat, 3 6.13]
apyevātikramed velāṃ sāgaro makarālayaḥ | [AvŚat, 3 6.14]
na tu vaineyavatsānāṃ buddho velām atikramet | [AvŚat, 3 6.15]
paśyati bhagavān ayaṃ dārakaḥ kusīdo maddarśanād vīryam ārapsyate yāvad anuttarāyāṃ samyaksaṃbodhau cittaṃ pariṇāmayiṣyatīti | [AvŚat, 3 7.1]
tato bhagavatā tīrthyānāṃ madadarpacchittyarthaṃ dārakasya ca kuśalamūlasaṃjananārthaṃ sūryasahasrātirekaprabhāḥ kanakavarṇamarīcaya utsṛṣṭāḥ yais tad gṛhaṃ samantād avabhāsitam | [AvŚat, 3 7.2]
kalpasahasraparibhāvitāś ca maitryaṃśava utsṛṣṭāḥ yair asya spṛṣṭamātraṃ śarīraṃ prahlāditam | [AvŚat, 3 7.3]
sa itaś cāmutaś ca prekṣitum ārabdhaḥ kasya prabhāvān mama śarīraṃ prahlāditam iti | [AvŚat, 3 7.4]
tato bhagavān bhikṣugaṇaparivṛtas tad gṛhaṃ praviveśa | [AvŚat, 3 7.5]
dadarśa kusīdo buddhaṃ bhagavantaṃ dvātriṃśatā mahāpuruṣalakṣaṇaiḥ samalaṃkṛtamaśītyā cānuvyañjanair virājitagātraṃ vyāmaprabhālaṃkṛtaṃ sūryasahasrātirekaprabhaṃ jaṅgamam iva ratnaparvataṃ samantato bhadrakam | [AvŚat, 3 7.6]
dṛṣṭvā ca punaḥ paraṃ prasādam āpannaḥ | [AvŚat, 3 7.7]
sahasā svayam evotthāya bhagavato 'rthe āsanaṃ prajñapayati | [AvŚat, 3 7.8]
evaṃ cāha etu bhagavān svāgataṃ bhagavataḥ niṣīdatu bhagavān prajñapta evāsana iti | [AvŚat, 3 7.9]
athāsya mātāpitarāv antarjanaś cādṛṣṭapūrvaprabhāvaṃ dṛṣṭvā paramaṃ vismayam āpannāḥ | [AvŚat, 3 7.10]
tataḥ kusīdo dārako harṣavikasitābhyāṃ nayanābhyāṃ bhagavataḥ pādābhivandanaṃ kṛtvā purastān niṣaṇṇo dharmaśravaṇāya | [AvŚat, 3 8.1]
tasmai bhagavatā anekaprakāraṃ kausīdyasyāvarṇo bhāṣitaḥ vīryārambhasya cānuśaṃsaḥ | [AvŚat, 3 8.2]
candanamayīṃ cāsya yaṣṭim anuprayacchati imāṃ dāraka yaṣṭim ākoṭayeti | [AvŚat, 3 8.3]
sa tām ākoṭayitum ārabdhaḥ | [AvŚat, 3 8.4]
athāsau yaṣṭir ākoṭyamānā manojñaśabdaśravaṇaṃ karoti vividhāni ca ratnanidhānāni paśyati | [AvŚat, 3 8.5]
tasyaitad abhavat mahān batāyaṃ vīryārambhe viśeṣo yannvahaṃ bhūyasyā mātrayā vīryam ārabheyeti | [AvŚat, 3 8.6]
sa śrāvastyāṃ ghaṇṭāvaghoṣaṇaṃ sārthavāham ātmānam udghoṣya ṣaḍvārān mahāsamudram avatīrṇaḥ | [AvŚat, 3 8.7]
tataḥ siddhayānapātreṇa mahāratnasaṃgrahaṃ kṛtvā bhagavān antarniveśane saśrāvakasaṃgho bhojitaḥ | [AvŚat, 3 8.8]
anuttarāyāṃ ca samyaksaṃbodhau praṇidhānaṃ kṛtam | [AvŚat, 3 8.9]
atha bhagavān kusīdasya dārakasya hetuparaṃparāṃ karmaparaṃparāṃ ca jñātvā smitaṃ prāvirakārṣīt | [AvŚat, 3 9.1]
dharmatā khalu yasmin samaye buddhā bhagavantaḥ smitaṃ prāviṣkurvanti tasmin samaye nīlapītalohitāvadātā arciṣo mukhān niścārya kāścid adhastād gacchanti kāścid upariṣṭād gacchanti | [AvŚat, 3 9.2]
yā adhastād gacchanti tāḥ saṃjīvaṃ kālasūtraṃ saṃghātaṃ rauravaṃ mahārauravaṃ tapanaṃ pratāpanam avīcim arbudaṃ nirarbudaṃ aṭaṭaṃ hahavaṃ huhuvam utpalaṃ padmaṃ mahāpadmaṃ narakān gatvā ye uṣṇanarakās teṣu śītībhūtā nipatanti ye śītanarakās teṣu uṣṇībhūtā nipatanti tena teṣāṃ sattvānāṃ kāraṇāviśeṣāḥ pratiprasrabhyante | [AvŚat, 3 9.3]
teṣām evaṃ bhavati kiṃ nu vayaṃ bhavanta itaś cyutāḥ āhosvid anyatropapannā iti | [AvŚat, 3 9.4]
teṣāṃ prasādasaṃjananārthaṃ bhagavān nirmitaṃ visarjayati | [AvŚat, 3 9.5]
teṣāṃ nirmitaṃ dṛṣṭvaivaṃ bhavati na hy eva vayaṃ bhavantaḥ itaś cyutāḥ nāpyanyatropapannāḥ | [AvŚat, 3 9.6]
api tv ayam apūrvadarśanaḥ sattvaḥ asyānubhāvenāsmākaṃ kāraṇāviśeṣāḥ pratiprasrabdhā iti | [AvŚat, 3 9.7]
te nirmite cittam abhiprasādya tan narakavedanīyaṃ karma kṣapayitvā devamanuṣyeṣu pratisandhiṃ gṛhṇanti yatra satyānāṃ bhājanabhūtā bhavanti | [AvŚat, 3 9.8]
yā upariṣṭād gacchanti tāś cāturmahārājikāṃs trayastriṃśān yāmāṃs tuṣitān nirmāṇaratīn paranirmitavaśavartino brahmakāyikān brahmapurohitān mahābrahmaṇaḥ parīttābhān apramāṇābhān ābhāsvarān parīttaśubhān apramāṇaśubhāñ śubhakṛtsnān anabhrakān puṇyaprasavān bṛhatphalān abṛhān atapān sudṛśān sudarśanān akaniṣṭhān devān gatvā anityaṃ duḥkhaṃ śūnyam anātmety udghoṣayanti gāthādvayaṃ ca bhāṣante | [AvŚat, 3 9.9]
ārabhadhvaṃ niṣkrāmata yujyadhvaṃ buddhaśāsane | [AvŚat, 3 9.10]
dhunīta mṛtyunaḥ sainyaṃ naḍāgāram iva kuñjaraḥ | [AvŚat, 3 9.11]
yo hy asmin dharmavinaye apramattaś cariṣyati | [AvŚat, 3 10.1]
prahāya jātisaṃsāraṃ duḥkhasyāntaṃ kariṣyati | [AvŚat, 3 10.2]
iti | [AvŚat, 3 10.3]
atha tā arciṣas trisāhasramahāsāhasraṃ lokadhātum anvāhiṇḍya bhagavantam eva pṛṣṭhataḥ pṛṣṭhataḥ samanugacchanti | [AvŚat, 3 11.1]
tad yadi bhagavān atītaṃ karma vyākartukāmo bhavati bhagavataḥ pṛṣṭhato 'ntardhīyante | [AvŚat, 3 11.2]
anāgataṃ vyākartukāmo bhavati purastād antardhīyante | [AvŚat, 3 11.3]
narakopapattiṃ vyākartukāmo bhavati pādatale 'ntardhīyante | [AvŚat, 3 11.4]
tiryagupapattiṃ vyākartukāmo bhavati pārṣṇyām antardhīyante | [AvŚat, 3 11.5]
pretopapattiṃ vyākartukāmo bhavati pādāṅguṣṭhe 'ntardhīyante | [AvŚat, 3 11.6]
manuṣyopapattiṃ vyākartukāmo bhavati jānunor antardhīyante | [AvŚat, 3 11.7]
balacakravartirājyaṃ vyākartukāmo bhavati vāme karatale 'ntardhīyante | [AvŚat, 3 11.8]
cakravartirājyaṃ vyākartukāmo bhavati dakṣiṇe karatale 'ntardhīyante | [AvŚat, 3 11.9]
devopapattiṃ vyākartukāmo bhavati nābhyām antardhīyante | [AvŚat, 3 11.10]
śrāvakabodhiṃ vyākartukāmo bhavati āsye 'ntardhīyante | [AvŚat, 3 11.11]
pratyekabodhiṃ vyākartukāmo bhavati ūrṇāyām antardhīyante | [AvŚat, 3 11.12]
anuttarāṃ samyaksaṃbodhiṃ vyākartukāmo bhavati uṣṇīṣe antardhīyante | [AvŚat, 3 11.13]
atha ca tā arciṣo bhagavantaṃ triḥ pradakṣiṇīkṛtya bhagavata uṣṇīṣe 'ntarhitāḥ | [AvŚat, 3 12.1]
athāyuṣmān ānandaḥ kṛtakarapuṭo bhagavantaṃ papraccha | [AvŚat, 3 12.2]
nānāvidho raṅgasahasracitro vaktrāntarān niṣkasitaḥ kalāpaḥ | [AvŚat, 3 12.3]
avabhāsitā yena diśaḥ samantād divākareṇodayatā yathaiva | [AvŚat, 3 12.4]
gāthāś ca bhāṣate | [AvŚat, 3 13.1]
vigatodbhavā dainyamadaprahīṇā buddhā jagaty uttamahetubhūtāḥ | [AvŚat, 3 13.2]
nākāraṇaṃ śaṅkhamṛṇālagauraṃ smitam upadarśayanti jinā jitārayaḥ | [AvŚat, 3 13.3]
tatkālaṃ svayam adhigamya vīra buddhyā śrotṝṇāṃ śramaṇa jinendra kāṅkṣitānām | [AvŚat, 3 14.1]
dhīrābhir munivṛṣa vāgbhir uttamābhir utpannaṃ vyapanaya saṃśayaṃ śubhābhiḥ | [AvŚat, 3 14.2]
nākasmāllavaṇajalādrirājadhairyāḥ saṃbuddhāḥ smitam upadarśayanti nāthāḥ | [AvŚat, 3 15.1]
yasyārthe smitam upadarśayanti dhīrāḥ taṃ śrotuṃ samabhilaṣanti te janaughāḥ | [AvŚat, 3 15.2]
iti | [AvŚat, 3 15.3]
bhagavān āha evam etad ānanda evam etat | [AvŚat, 3 16.1]
nāhetvapratyayam ānanda tathāgatā arhantaḥ samyaksaṃbuddhāḥ smitaṃ prāviṣkurvanti | [AvŚat, 3 16.2]
paśyasy ānanda anena kusīdena dārakeṇa mamaivaṃvidhaṃ satkāraṃ kṛtam | [AvŚat, 3 16.3]
evaṃ bhadanta | [AvŚat, 3 16.4]
eṣa ānanda kusīdo dārako 'nena kuśalamūlena cittotpādena deyadharmaparityāgena ca trikalpāsaṃkhyeyasamudānītāṃ bodhiṃ samudānīya mahākaruṇāparibhāvitāḥ ṣaṭpāramitāḥ paripūrya atibalavīryaparākramo nāma samyaksaṃbuddho bhaviṣyati daśabhir balaiś caturbhir vaiśāradyais tribhir āveṇikaiḥ smṛtyupasthānair mahākaruṇayā ca | [AvŚat, 3 16.5]
ayam asya deyadharmo yo mamāntike cittaprasāda iti | [AvŚat, 3 16.6]
idam avocad bhagavān | [AvŚat, 3 17.1]
āttamanasas te ca bhikṣavo bhagavato bhāṣitam abhyanandan | [AvŚat, 3 17.2]
{AvŚat, 4}
buddho bhagavān satkṛto gurukṛto mānitaḥ pūjito rājabhī rājamātrair dhanibhiḥ pauraiḥ śreṣṭhibhiḥ sārthavāhair devair nāgair yakṣair asurair garuḍaiḥ kinnarair mahoragair iti devanāgayakṣāsuragaruḍakinnaramahoragābhyarcito buddho bhagavān jñāto mahāpuṇyo lābhī cīvarapiṇḍapātaśayanāsanaglānapratyayabhaiṣajyapariṣkārāṇāṃ saśrāvakasaṃghaḥ śrāvastyāṃ viharati jetavane 'nāthapiṇḍadasyārāme | [AvŚat, 4 1.1]
śrāvastyām anyatamo mahāsārthavāho mahāsamudrād bhagnayānapātra āgataḥ | [AvŚat, 4 2.1]
sa dvir api trir api svadevatāyācanaṃ kṛtvā mahāsamudram avatīrṇo bhagnayānapātra evāgataḥ | [AvŚat, 4 2.2]
tato 'sya mahān kheda utpannaḥ | [AvŚat, 4 2.3]
sa imāṃ cintām āpede ko me upāyaḥ syādyena dhanārjanaṃ kuryām iti | [AvŚat, 4 2.4]
tasyaitad abhavat ayaṃ buddho bhagavān sarvadevaprativiśiṣṭataraḥ ātmahitaparahitapratipannaḥ kāruṇiko mahādharmakāmaḥ prajāvatsalaḥ yannvaham idānīm asya nāmnā punar api mahāsamudram avatareyam | [AvŚat, 4 2.5]
siddhayānapātras tv āgaccheyaṃ ced upārdhena dhanenāsya pūjāṃ kuryām iti | [AvŚat, 4 2.6]
sa evaṃ kṛtavyavasāyaḥ punar api mahāsamudram avatīrṇaḥ | [AvŚat, 4 3.1]
buddhānubhāvena ca ratnadvīpaṃ samprāpya mahāratnasaṃgrahaṃ kṛtvā kuśalasvastinā svagṛham anuprāptaḥ | [AvŚat, 4 3.2]
sa mārgaśramaṃ prativinodya bhāṇḍaṃ pratyavekṣitum ārabdhaḥ | [AvŚat, 4 3.3]
tasya nānāvicitrāṇi ratnāni dṛṣṭvā mahāṃllābha utpannaḥ | [AvŚat, 4 3.4]
cintayati ca mayā īdṛśānāṃ ratnānāṃ śramaṇasya gautamasya upārdhaṃ dātavyaṃ bhaviṣyati | [AvŚat, 4 3.5]
yannvaham etāni svasyāḥ patnyā āyaḥ | [AvŚat, 4 3.6]
tena kārṣāpaṇadvayena vikrīya bhagavato gandhaṃ dadyām iti | [AvŚat, 4 3.7]
sa kārṣāpaṇadvayenāgaruṃ krītvā jetavanaṃ gataḥ | [AvŚat, 4 3.8]
tato 'patrapamāṇarūpo dvārakoṣṭhake sthitvāgaruṃ dhūpitavān | [AvŚat, 4 3.9]
atha bhagavāṃstad rūpam ṛddhyabhisaṃskāram abhisaṃskṛtavān yena sa dhūpa upari vihāyasam abhyudgamya sarvāṃ ca śrāvastīṃ sphuritvā mahadabhrakūṭavad avasthitaḥ | [AvŚat, 4 4.1]
tasya tad atyadbhutaṃ devamanuṣyāvarjanakaraṃ prātihāryaṃ dṛṣṭvā mahān prasāda utpannaḥ | [AvŚat, 4 4.2]
sa svacittaṃ paribhāṣitavān naitan mama pratirūpaṃ syād yad ahaṃ bhagavantaṃ ratnair nābhyarcayeyam iti | [AvŚat, 4 4.3]
atha tena sārthavāhena bhagavān saśrāvakasaṃgho 'ntarniveśane bhaktenopanimantritaḥ | [AvŚat, 4 5.1]
tataḥ praṇītenāhāreṇa saṃtarpya mahāratnair avakīrṇaḥ | [AvŚat, 4 5.2]
tatas tāni ratnāni upari vihāyasam abhyudgamya mūrdhni bhagavato ratnakūṭāgāro ratnacchatraṃ ratnamaṇḍapaś cāvasthitaḥ yan na śakyaṃ suśikṣitena karmakāreṇa karmāntevāsinā vā kartum yathāpi tad buddhasya buddhānubhāvena devatānāṃ ca devatānubhāvena | [AvŚat, 4 5.3]
atha sārthavāho dviguṇajātaprasādas tatpratihāryadarśanān mūlanikṛtta iva drumo bhagavataḥ pādayor nipatya praṇidhānaṃ kartum ārabdhaḥ anenāhaṃ kuśalamūlena cittotpādena deyadharmaparityāgena ca andhe loke anāyake apariṇāyake buddho bhūyāsam atīrṇānāṃ sattvānāṃ tārayitā amuktānāṃ mocayitā anāśvastānām āśvāsayitā aparinirvṛtānāṃ parinirvāpayiteti | [AvŚat, 4 6.1]
atha bhagavāṃs tasya sārthavāhasya hetuparaṃparāṃ karmaparaṃparāṃ ca jñātvā smitaṃ prāviṣkārṣīt | [AvŚat, 4 7.1]
dharmatā khalu yasmin samaye buddhā bhagavantaḥ smitaṃ prāviṣkurvanti tasmin samaye nīlapītalohitāvadātā arciṣo mukhān niścārya kāścid adhastād gacchanti kāścid upariṣṭād gacchanti | [AvŚat, 4 7.2]
yā adhastād gacchanti tāḥ saṃjīvaṃ kālasūtraṃ saṃghātaṃ rauravaṃ mahārauravaṃ tapanaṃ pratāpanam avīcim arbudaṃ nirarbudaṃ aṭaṭaṃ hahavaṃ huhuvam utpalaṃ padmaṃ mahāpadmaṃ narakān gatvā ye uṣṇanarakās teṣu śītībhūtā nipatanti ye śītanarakās teṣūṣṇībhūtā nipatanti | [AvŚat, 4 7.3]
tena teṣāṃ sattvānāṃ kāraṇāviśeṣāḥ pratiprasrabhyante | [AvŚat, 4 7.4]
teṣām evaṃ bhavati kiṃ nu vayaṃ bhavanta itaś cyutāḥ āhosvid anyatropapannā iti | [AvŚat, 4 7.5]
teṣāṃ prasādasaṃjananārthaṃ bhagavān nirmitaṃ visarjayati | [AvŚat, 4 7.6]
teṣāṃ nirmitaṃ dṛṣṭvaivaṃ bhavati na hy eva vayaṃ bhavantaḥ itaś cyutā nāpy anyatropapannāḥ | [AvŚat, 4 7.7]
api tv ayam apūrvadarśanaḥ sattvaḥ asyānubhāvenāsmākaṃ kāraṇāviśeṣāḥ pratiprasrabdhā iti | [AvŚat, 4 7.8]
te nirmite cittam abhiprasādya tan narakavedanīyaṃ karma kṣapayitvā devamanuṣyeṣu pratisandhiṃ gṛhṇanti yatra satyānāṃ bhājanabhūtā bhavanti | [AvŚat, 4 7.9]
yā upariṣṭād gacchanti tāś cāturmahārājikāṃs trayastriṃśān yāmāṃs tuṣitān nirmāṇaratīn paranirmitavaśavartino brahmakāyikān brahmapurohitān mahābrahmaṇaḥ parīttābhān apramāṇābhān ābhāsvarān parīttaśubhān apramāṇaśubhāñ śubhakṛtsnān anabhrakān puṇyaprasavān bṛhatphalān abṛhān atapān sudṛśān sudarśanān akaniṣṭhān devān gatvā anityaṃ duḥkhaṃ śūnyam anātmety udghoṣayanti gāthādvayaṃ ca bhāṣante | [AvŚat, 4 7.10]
ārabhadhvaṃ niṣkrāmata yujyadhvaṃ buddhaśāsane | [AvŚat, 4 7.11]
dhunīta mṛtyunaḥ sainyaṃ naḍāgāram iva kuñjaraḥ | [AvŚat, 4 7.12]
yo hy asmin dharmavinaye apramattaś cariṣyati | [AvŚat, 4 8.1]
prahāya jātisaṃsāraṃ duḥkhasyāntaṃ kariṣyati | [AvŚat, 4 8.2]
iti | [AvŚat, 4 8.3]
atha tā arciṣas trisāhasramahāsāhasraṃ lokadhātum anvāhiṇḍya bhagavantam eva pṛṣṭhataḥ pṛṣṭhataḥ samanugacchanti | [AvŚat, 4 9.1]
tad yadi bhagavān atītaṃ karma vyākartukāmo bhavati bhagavataḥ pṛṣṭhato 'ntardhīyante | [AvŚat, 4 9.2]
anāgataṃ vyākartukāmo bhavati purastād antardhīyante | [AvŚat, 4 9.3]
narakopapattiṃ vyākartukāmo bhavati pādatale 'ntardhīyante | [AvŚat, 4 9.4]
tiryagupapattiṃ vyākartukāmo bhavati pārṣṇyām antardhīyante | [AvŚat, 4 9.5]
pretopapattiṃ vyākartukāmo bhavati pādāṅguṣṭhe 'ntardhīyante | [AvŚat, 4 9.6]
manuṣyopapattiṃ vyākartukāmo bhavati jānunor antardhīyante | [AvŚat, 4 9.7]
balacakravartirājyaṃ vyākartukāmo bhavati vāme karatale 'ntardhīyante | [AvŚat, 4 9.8]
cakravartirājyaṃ vyākartukāmo bhavati dakṣiṇe karatale 'ntardhīyante | [AvŚat, 4 9.9]
devopapattiṃ vyākartukāmo bhavati nābhyām antardhīyante | [AvŚat, 4 9.10]
śrāvakabodhiṃ vyākartukāmo bhavati āsye 'ntardhīyante | [AvŚat, 4 9.11]
pratyekabodhiṃ vyākartukāmo bhavati ūrṇāyām antardhīyante | [AvŚat, 4 9.12]
anuttarāṃ samyaksaṃbodhiṃ vyākartukāmo bhavati uṣṇīṣe antardhīyante | [AvŚat, 4 9.13]
atha tā arciṣo bhagavantaṃ triḥ pradakṣiṇīkṛtya bhagavata uṣṇīṣe 'ntarhitāḥ | [AvŚat, 4 10.1]
athāyuṣmān ānandaḥ kṛtakarapuṭo bhagavantaṃ papraccha | [AvŚat, 4 10.2]
nānāvidho raṅgasahasracitro vaktrāntarān niṣkasitaḥ kalāpaḥ | [AvŚat, 4 10.3]
avabhāsitā yena diśaḥ samantād divākareṇodayatā yathaiva | [AvŚat, 4 10.4]
gāthāś ca bhāṣate | [AvŚat, 4 11.1]
vigatodbhavā dainyamadaprahīṇā buddhā jagaty uttamahetubhūtāḥ | [AvŚat, 4 11.2]
nākāraṇaṃ śaṅkhamṛṇālagauraṃ smitam upadarśayanti jinā jitārayaḥ | [AvŚat, 4 11.3]
tatkālaṃ svayam adhigamya vīra buddhyā śrotṝṇāṃ śramaṇa jinendra kāṅkṣitānām | [AvŚat, 4 12.1]
dhīrābhir munivṛṣa vāgbhir uttamābhir utpannaṃ vyapanaya saṃśayaṃ śubhābhiḥ | [AvŚat, 4 12.2]
nākasmāl lavaṇajalādrirājadhairyāḥ saṃbuddhāḥ smitam upadarśayanti nāthāḥ | [AvŚat, 4 13.1]
yasyārthe smitam upadarśayanti dhīrāḥ taṃ śrotuṃ samabhilaṣanti te janaughāḥ | [AvŚat, 4 13.2]
iti | [AvŚat, 4 13.3]
bhagavān āha evam etad ānanda evam etat | [AvŚat, 4 14.1]
nāhetvapratyayam ānanda tathāgatā arhantaḥ samyaksaṃbuddhāḥ smitaṃ prāviṣkurvanti | [AvŚat, 4 14.2]
paśyasy ānanda anena sārthavāhena mamaivaṃvidhaṃ satkāraṃ kṛtam | [AvŚat, 4 14.3]
evaṃ bhadanta | [AvŚat, 4 14.4]
eṣa ānanda sārthavāho 'nena kuśalamūlena cittotpādena deyadharmaparityāgena ca trikalpāsaṃkhyeyasamudānītāṃ bodhiṃ samudānīya mahākaruṇāparibhāvitāḥ ṣaṭ pāramitāḥ paripūrya ratnottamo nāma samyaksaṃbuddho bhaviṣyati daśabhir balaiś caturbhir vaiśāradyais tribhir āveṇikaiḥ smṛtyupasthānair mahākaruṇayā ca | [AvŚat, 4 14.5]
ayam asya deyadharmo yo mamāntike cittasyābhiprasādaḥ | [AvŚat, 4 14.6]
idam avocad bhagavān | [AvŚat, 4 15.1]
āttamanasas te bhikṣavo bhagavato bhāṣitam abhyanandan | [AvŚat, 4 15.2]
{AvŚat, 6}
buddho bhagavān satkṛto gurukṛto mānitaḥ pūjito rājabhī rājamātrair dhanibhiḥ pauraiḥ śreṣṭhibhiḥ sārthavāhair devair nāgair yakṣair asurair garuḍaiḥ kinnarair mahoragair iti devanāgayakṣāsuragaruḍakinnaramahoragābhyarcito buddho bhagavān jñāto mahāpuṇyo lābhī cīvarapiṇḍapātaśayanāsanaglānapratyayabhaiṣajyapariṣkārāṇāṃ saśrāvakasaṃghaḥ śrāvastyāṃ viharati jetavane 'nāthapiṇḍadasyārāme | [AvŚat, 6 1.1]
śrāvastyām anyatamo gṛhapatiḥ śreṣṭhī prativasati āḍhyo mahādhano mahābhogo vistīrṇaviśālaparigraho vaiśravaṇadhanasamudito vaiśravaṇadhanapratispardhī | [AvŚat, 6 2.1]
tena sadṛśāt kulāt kalatram ānītam | [AvŚat, 6 2.2]
sa tayā sārdhaṃ krīḍati ramate paricārayati | [AvŚat, 6 2.3]
tasya krīḍato ramamāṇasya paricārayataḥ gṛhapateḥ patnī āpannasattvā saṃvṛttā | [AvŚat, 6 2.4]
sā navānāṃ māsānām atyayāt prasūtā | [AvŚat, 6 2.5]
dārako jāto abhirūpo darśanīyaḥ prāsādikaḥ | [AvŚat, 6 2.6]
tasya jātau jātimahaṃ kṛtvā vaḍika iti nāmadheyaṃ kṛtavān pitā | [AvŚat, 6 3.1]
vaḍiko dārako 'ṣṭābhyo dhātrībhyo dattaḥ aṃsadhātrībhyāṃ kṣīradhātrībhyāṃ maladhātrībhyāṃ krīḍanikābhyāṃ dhātrībhyām | [AvŚat, 6 3.2]
so 'ṣṭābhir dhātrībhir unnīyate vardhyate kṣīreṇa dadhnā navanītena sarpiṣā sarpimaṇḍena anyaiś cottaptottaptair upakaraṇaviśeṣaiḥ | [AvŚat, 6 3.3]
āśu vardhate hradastham iva paṅkajam | [AvŚat, 6 3.4]
yadā mahān saṃvṛttaḥ pañcavarṣaḥ ṣaḍvarṣo vā tadā gurau bhaktiṃ kṛtvā sarvaśāstrāṇi adhītāni | [AvŚat, 6 3.5]
tīkṣṇabuddhitayā śīghraṃ sarvaśāstrasya pāraṃ gataḥ | [AvŚat, 6 3.6]
tad anantaraṃ tasya vaḍikasya kiṃcit pūrvajanmakṛtakarmavipākena śarīre kāyikaṃ duḥkhaṃ patitam iti duḥkhī bhūtaś cintāparaḥ sthitaḥ kiṃ pāpaṃ kṛtaṃ mayā yad idaṃ kāyikaṃ duḥkhaṃ mama śarīre jātam | [AvŚat, 6 4.1]
tataḥ sa vaidyas tasya rogacihnaṃ dṛṣṭvā cikitsāṃ kartum ārabdhaḥ | [AvŚat, 6 4.2]
tathāpi tasya rogaśāntir na bhavati punar vṛddhir bhavati | [AvŚat, 6 4.3]
pitā putrasya rogaṃ vṛddhaṃ jātaṃ dṛṣṭvā avaśyaṃ putro mariṣyati yad vaidyenāpi cāsya rogasya cikitsituṃ na śakyate iti mūrcchayā bhūmau patitaḥ | [AvŚat, 6 4.4]
taṃ dṛṣṭvā bhūyo 'pi putrasya cintā jātā | [AvŚat, 6 4.5]
bhūyo 'pi cintayā mānasī vyathā jātā | [AvŚat, 6 4.6]
sa dārako rogī bhūto 'śakyo 'pi vadituṃ kathaṃcit pitaraṃ babhāṣe mā tāta sāhasam | [AvŚat, 6 4.7]
dhairyam avalambyottiṣṭha | [AvŚat, 6 4.8]
mamātyayāśaṅkayā mā bhūs tvam api mādṛśaḥ | [AvŚat, 6 4.9]
mama nāmnā devānāṃ pūjāṃ kuru dānaṃ dehi | [AvŚat, 6 4.10]
tato mama svasthā bhaviṣyati | [AvŚat, 6 4.11]
sa gṛhapatir iti putrasya vaca ākarṇya sarvadevebhyaḥ pūjāṃ kṛtavān | [AvŚat, 6 4.12]
sarvabrāhmaṇatīrthikaparivrājakebhyo dānaṃ dattavān | [AvŚat, 6 4.13]
tathāpi tasya rogaśāntir na bhavati | [AvŚat, 6 4.14]
tadā tasya mahān mānaso duḥkho 'bhūt | [AvŚat, 6 4.15]
sarvadeveṣu pūjā kṛtā dāno 'pi dattaḥ pitrā mama tathāpi svasthā na bhavati | [AvŚat, 6 4.16]
tatas tathāgataguṇān anusmṛtya buddhaṃ namaskāraṃ kartum ārabdhaḥ | [AvŚat, 6 4.17]
atrāntare nāsti kiṃcid buddhānāṃ bhagavatām ajñātam adṛṣṭam aviditam avijñātam | [AvŚat, 6 4.18]
dharmatā khalu buddhānāṃ bhagavatāṃ mahākāruṇikānāṃ lokānugrahapravṛttakānām ekārakṣāṇāṃ śamathavipaśyanāvihāriṇāṃ tridamathavastukuśalānāṃ caturoghottīrṇānāṃ caturṛddhipādacaraṇatalasupratiṣṭhitānāṃ caturṣu saṃgrahavastuṣu dīrgharātrakṛtaparicayānāṃ pañcāṅgaviprahīṇānāṃ pañcagatisamatikrāntānāṃ ṣaḍaṅgasamanvāgatānāṃ ṣaṭpāramitāparipūrṇānāṃ saptabodhyaṅgakusumāḍhyānām aṣṭāṅgamārgadeśikānāṃ navānupūrvavihārasamāpattikuśalānāṃ daśabalabalināṃ daśadiksamāpūrṇayaśasāṃ daśaśatavaśavartiprativiśiṣṭānāṃ trī rātres trir divasasya ca buddhacakṣuṣā lokaṃ vyavalokya jñānadarśanaṃ pravartate ko hīyate ko vardhate kaḥ kṛcchraprāptaḥ kaḥ saṃkaṭaprāptaḥ kaḥ saṃbādhaprāptaḥ kaḥ kṛcchrasaṃkaṭasaṃbādhaprāptaḥ ko 'pāyanimnaḥ ko 'pāyapravaṇaḥ ko 'pāyaprāgbhāraḥ kam aham apāyād uddhṛtya svarge mokṣe ca pratiṣṭhāpayeyam | [AvŚat, 6 4.19]
kasya kāmapaṅkanimagnasya hastoddhāram anupradadyām | [AvŚat, 6 4.20]
kam āryadhanavirahitam āryadhanaiśvaryādhipatye pratiṣṭhāpayeyam | [AvŚat, 6 4.21]
kasyājñānatimirapaṭalaparyavanaddhanetrasya jñānāñjanaśalākayā cakṣur viśodhayāmi | [AvŚat, 6 4.22]
kasyānavaropitāni kuśalamūlāny avaropayeyam | [AvŚat, 6 4.23]
kasyāvaropitāni paripācayeyam | [AvŚat, 6 4.24]
kasya paripakvāni vimocayeyam | [AvŚat, 6 4.25]
āha ca | [AvŚat, 6 4.26]
apy evātikramed velāṃ sāgaro makarālayaḥ | [AvŚat, 6 4.27]
na tu vaineyavatsānāṃ buddho velām atikramet | [AvŚat, 6 4.28]
tato bhagavatā vaḍikasya gṛhapateḥ putrasya tām avasthāṃ dṛṣṭvā sūryasahasrātirekaprabhāḥ kanakavarṇā marīcayaḥ sṛṣṭāḥ yais tad gṛhaṃ samantād avabhāsitam | [AvŚat, 6 5.1]
kalpasahasraparibhāvitāś ca maitryaṃśava utsṛṣṭāḥ yair asya spṛṣṭamātraṃ śarīraṃ prahlāditam | [AvŚat, 6 5.2]
tato bhagavāṃs tasya dvārakoṣṭhakam anuprāptaḥ | [AvŚat, 6 5.3]
dauvārikapuruṣeṇāsya niveditaṃ bhagavān dvāre tiṣṭhatīti | [AvŚat, 6 5.4]
atha vaḍikaḥ śreṣṭhiputro labdhaprasādo 'dhigatasamāśvāsa āha praviśatu bhagavān svāgataṃ bhagavate ākāṅkṣāmi bhagavato darśanam iti | [AvŚat, 6 5.5]
atha bhagavān praviśya prajñapta evāsane niṣaṇṇaḥ | [AvŚat, 6 5.6]
niṣadya bhagavān vaḍikam uvāca kiṃ te vaḍika bādhata iti | [AvŚat, 6 5.7]
vaḍika uvāca kāyikaṃ ca me duḥkhaṃ cetasikaṃ ceti | [AvŚat, 6 5.8]
tato 'sya bhagavatā sarvasatveṣu maitryupadiṣṭā ayaṃ te cetasikasya pratipakṣa iti | [AvŚat, 6 5.9]
laukikaṃ ca cittam utpādayāmāsa aho bata śakro devendro gandhamādanāt parvatāt kṣīrikām oṣadhīm ānayed iti | [AvŚat, 6 5.10]
sahacittotpādād bhagavataḥ śakro devendro gandhamādanāt parvatāt kṣīrikām oṣadhīm ānīya bhagavate dattavān | [AvŚat, 6 5.11]
bhagavatā ca svapāṇinā gṛhītvā vaḍikāya dattā iyaṃ te kāyikasya duḥkhasya paridāhaśamanīti | [AvŚat, 6 5.12]
sa kāyikaṃ prasrabdhisukhaṃ labdhvā bhagavato 'ntike cittaṃ prasādayāmāsa | [AvŚat, 6 6.1]
prasannacittaś ca rājñaḥ prasenajito nivedya bhagavantaṃ saśrāvakasaṃghaṃ bhojayitvā śatasahasreṇa vastreṇācchādya sarvapuṣpamālyair abhyarcitavān | [AvŚat, 6 6.2]
tataś cetanāṃ puṣṇāti sma praṇidhiṃ ca cakāra anenāhaṃ kuśalamūlena cittotpādena deyadharmaparityāgena yathaivāhaṃ bhagavatā anuttareṇa vaidyarājena cikitsitaḥ evam aham apy anāgate 'dhvani andhe loke anāyake apariṇāyake buddho bhūyāsam atīrṇānāṃ sattvānāṃ tārayitā amuktānāṃ mocayitā anāśvastānām āśvāsayitā aparinirvṛtānāṃ parinirvāpayiteti | [AvŚat, 6 6.3]
atha bhagavān vaḍikasya dhātuparaṃparāṃ karmaparaṃparāṃ ca jñātvā smitaṃ prāvirakārṣīt | [AvŚat, 6 7.1]
dharmatā khalu yasmin samaye buddhā bhagavantaḥ smitaṃ prāviṣkurvanti tasmin samaye nīlapītalohitāvadātā arciṣo mukhān niścārya kāścid adhastād gacchanti kāścid upariṣṭād gacchanti | [AvŚat, 6 7.2]
yā adhastād gacchanti tāḥ saṃjīvaṃ kālasūtraṃ saṃghātaṃ rauravaṃ mahārauravaṃ tapanaṃ pratāpanam avīcim arbudaṃ nirarbudaṃ aṭaṭaṃ hahavaṃ huhuvam utpalaṃ padmaṃ mahāpadmaṃ narakān gatvā ye uṣṇanarakās teṣu śītībhūtā nipatanti ye śītanarakās teṣu uṣṇībhūtā nipatanti tena teṣāṃ sattvānāṃ kāraṇāviśeṣāḥ pratiprasrabhyante | [AvŚat, 6 7.3]
teṣām evaṃ bhavati kiṃ nu vayaṃ bhavanta itaś cyutāḥ āhosvid anyatropapannā iti | [AvŚat, 6 7.4]
teṣāṃ prasādasaṃjananārthaṃ bhagavān nirmitaṃ visarjayati | [AvŚat, 6 7.5]
teṣāṃ nirmitaṃ dṛṣṭvaivaṃ bhavati na hy eva vayaṃ bhavantaḥ itaś cyutāḥ nāpy anyatropapannāḥ | [AvŚat, 6 7.6]
api tv ayam apūrvadarśanaḥ sattvaḥ asyānubhāvenāsmākaṃ kāraṇāviśeṣāḥ pratiprasrabhyante | [AvŚat, 6 7.7]
te nirmite cittam abhiprasādya tan narakavedanīyaṃ karma kṣapayitvā devamanuṣyeṣu pratisandhiṃ gṛhṇanti yatra satyānāṃ bhājanabhūtā bhavanti | [AvŚat, 6 7.8]
yā upariṣṭād gacchanti tāś cāturmahārājikāṃs trayastriṃśān yāmāṃs tuṣitān nirmāṇaratīn paranirmitavaśavartino brahmakāyikān brahmapurohitān mahābrahmaṇaḥ parīttābhān apramāṇābhān ābhāsvarān parīttaśubhān apramāṇaśubhāñ śubhakṛtsnān anabhrakān puṇyaprasavān bṛhatphalān abṛhān atapān sudṛśān sudarśanān akaniṣṭhān devān gatvā anityaṃ duḥkhaṃ śūnyam anātmety udghoṣayanti gāthādvayaṃ ca bhāṣante | [AvŚat, 6 7.9]
ārabhadhvaṃ niṣkrāmata yujyadhvaṃ buddhaśāsane | [AvŚat, 6 7.10]
dhunīta mṛtyunaḥ sainyaṃ naḍāgāram iva kuñjaraḥ | [AvŚat, 6 7.11]
yo hy asmin dharmavinaye apramattaś cariṣyati | [AvŚat, 6 8.1]
prahāya jātisaṃsāraṃ duḥkhasyāntaṃ kariṣyati | [AvŚat, 6 8.2]
atha tā arciṣas trisāhasramahāsāhasraṃ lokadhātum anvāhiṇḍya bhagavantam eva pṛṣṭhataḥ pṛṣṭhataḥ samanugacchanti | [AvŚat, 6 9.1]
tad yadi bhagavān atītaṃ karma vyākartukāmo bhavati bhagavataḥ pṛṣṭhato 'ntardhīyante | [AvŚat, 6 9.2]
anāgataṃ vyākartukāmo bhavati purastād antardhīyante | [AvŚat, 6 9.3]
narakopapattiṃ vyākartukāmo bhavati pādatale 'ntardhīyante | [AvŚat, 6 9.4]
tiryagupapattiṃ vyākartukāmo bhavati pārṣṇyām antardhīyante | [AvŚat, 6 9.5]
pretopapattiṃ vyākartukāmo bhavati pādāṅguṣṭhe 'ntardhīyante | [AvŚat, 6 9.6]
manuṣyopapattiṃ vyākartukāmo bhavati jānunor antardhīyante | [AvŚat, 6 9.7]
balacakravartirājyaṃ vyākartukāmo bhavati vāme karatale 'ntardhīyante | [AvŚat, 6 9.8]
cakravartirājyaṃ vyākartukāmo bhavati dakṣiṇe karatale 'ntardhīyante | [AvŚat, 6 9.9]
devopapattiṃ vyākartukāmo bhavati nābhyām antardhīyante | [AvŚat, 6 9.10]
śrāvakabodhiṃ vyākartukāmo bhavati āsye 'ntardhīyante | [AvŚat, 6 9.11]
pratyekabodhiṃ vyākartukāmo bhavati ūrṇāyām antardhīyante | [AvŚat, 6 9.12]
anuttarāṃ samyaksaṃbodhiṃ vyākartukāmo bhavati uṣṇīṣe antardhīyante | [AvŚat, 6 9.13]
atha ca tā arciṣo bhagavantaṃ triḥ pradakṣiṇīkṛtya bhagavata uṣṇīṣe 'ntarhitāḥ | [AvŚat, 6 10.1]
athāyuṣmān ānandaḥ kṛtakarapuṭo bhagavantaṃ papraccha | [AvŚat, 6 10.2]
nānāvidho raṅgasahasracitro vaktrāntarān niṣkasitaḥ kalāpaḥ | [AvŚat, 6 10.3]
avabhāsitā yena diśaḥ samantād divākareṇodayatā yathaiva | [AvŚat, 6 10.4]
gāthāś ca bhāṣate | [AvŚat, 6 11.1]
vigatodbhavā dainyamadaprahīṇā buddhā jagaty uttamahetubhūtāḥ | [AvŚat, 6 11.2]
nākāraṇaṃ śaṅkhamṛṇālagauraṃ smitam upadarśayanti jinā jitārayaḥ | [AvŚat, 6 11.3]
tatkālaṃ svayam adhigamya dhīra buddhyā śrotṝṇāṃ śramaṇa jinendra kāṅkṣitānām | [AvŚat, 6 12.1]
dhīrābhir munivṛṣa vāgbhir uttamābhir utpannaṃ vyapanaya saṃśayaṃ śubhābhiḥ | [AvŚat, 6 12.2]
nākasmāllavaṇajalādrirājadhairyāḥ saṃbuddhāḥ smitam upadarśayanti nāthāḥ | [AvŚat, 6 13.1]
yasyārthe smitam upadarśayanti dhīrāḥ taṃ śrotuṃ samabhilaṣanti te janaughāḥ | [AvŚat, 6 13.2]
bhagavān āha evam etad ānanda evam etat | [AvŚat, 6 14.1]
nāhetvapratyayam ānanda tathāgatā arhantaḥ samyaksaṃbuddhāḥ smitaṃ prāviṣkurvanti | [AvŚat, 6 14.2]
paśyasy anena vaḍikena gṛhapatiputreṇa mamaivaṃvidhaṃ satkāraṃ kṛtam | [AvŚat, 6 14.3]
evaṃ bhadanta | [AvŚat, 6 14.4]
eṣa ānanda vaḍiko gṛhapatiputro 'nena kuśalamūlena cittotpādena deyadharmaparityāgena ca trikalpāsaṃkhyeyasamudānītāṃ bodhiṃ samudānīya mahākaruṇāparibhāvitāḥ ṣaṭ pāramitāḥ paripūrya śākyamunir nāma samyaksaṃbuddho bhaviṣyati daśabhir balaiś caturbhir vaiśāradyais tribhir āveṇikaiḥ smṛtyupasthānair mahākaruṇayā ca | [AvŚat, 6 14.5]
ayam asya deyadharmo yo mamāntike cittaprasāda iti | [AvŚat, 6 14.6]
idam avocad bhagavān | [AvŚat, 6 15.1]
āttamanasas te ca bhikṣavo bhagavato bhāṣitam abhyanandan | [AvŚat, 6 15.2]
{AvŚat, 7}
buddho bhagavān satkṛto gurukṛto mānitaḥ pūjito rājabhī rājamātrair dhanibhiḥ pauraiḥ śreṣṭhibhiḥ sārthavāhair devair nāgair yakṣair asurair garuḍaiḥ kinnarair mahoragair iti devanāgayakṣāsuragaruḍakinnaramahoragābhyarcito buddho bhagavān jñāto mahāpuṇyo lābhī cīvarapiṇḍapātaśayanāsanaglānapratyayabhaiṣajyapariṣkārāṇāṃ saśrāvakasaṃghaḥ śrāvastyāṃ viharati jetavane 'nāthapiṇḍadasyārāme | [AvŚat, 7 1.1]
yadā bhagavāṃl loke notpanna āsīt tadā rājā prasenajit tīrthikadevatārcanaṃ kṛtavān puṣpadhūpagandhamālyavilepanaiḥ | [AvŚat, 7 2.1]
yadā tu bhagavāṃl loke utpannaḥ rājā ca prasenajid daharasūtrodāharaṇena vinīto bhagavacchāsane śraddhāṃ pratilabdhavān tadā prītisaumanasyajātas trir bhagavantam upasaṃkramya dīpadhūpagandhamālyavilepanair abhyarcayati | [AvŚat, 7 2.2]
athānyatama ārāmiko navaṃ padmam ādāya rājñaḥ prasenajito 'rthaṃ śrāvastīṃ praviśati | [AvŚat, 7 3.1]
tīrthikopāsakena ca dṛṣṭaḥ pṛṣṭaś ca kim idaṃ padmaṃ vikrīṇīṣe sa kathayati āmeti | [AvŚat, 7 3.2]
sa kretukāmo yāvad anāthapiṇḍado gṛhapatis taṃ pradeśam anuprāptaḥ | [AvŚat, 7 3.3]
tena tasmād dviguṇena mūlyena vardhitam | [AvŚat, 7 4.1]
tataḥ parasparaṃ vardhamānau yāvacchatasahasraṃ vardhitavantau | [AvŚat, 7 4.2]
athārāmikasyaitad abhavat ayam anāthapiṇḍado gṛhapatir acañcalaḥ sthirasattvaḥ | [AvŚat, 7 4.3]
nūnam atra kāraṇena bhavitavyam iti | [AvŚat, 7 4.4]
tena saṃśayajātena sa tīrthikābhiprasannaḥ puruṣaḥ pṛṣṭaḥ kasyārthe bhavān evaṃ vardhata iti | [AvŚat, 7 4.5]
sa āha ahaṃ bhagavato nārāyaṇasyārthe iti | [AvŚat, 7 4.6]
anāthapiṇḍada āha ahaṃ bhagavato buddhasyārthe iti | [AvŚat, 7 5.1]
ārāmika āha ka eṣa buddho nāmeti tato 'nāthapiṇḍadena vistareṇāsya buddhaguṇā ākhyātāḥ | [AvŚat, 7 5.2]
tata ārāmiko 'nāthapiṇḍadam āha gṛhapate ahaṃ svayam eva taṃ bhagavantam abhyarcayiṣya iti | [AvŚat, 7 5.3]
tato 'nāthapiṇḍado gṛhapatir ārāmikam ādāya yena bhagavāṃs tenopasaṃkrāntaḥ | [AvŚat, 7 6.1]
dadarśārāmiko buddhaṃ bhagavantaṃ dvātriṃśatā mahāpuruṣalakṣaṇaiḥ samalaṃkṛtam aśītyā cānuvyañjanair virājitagātraṃ vyāmaprabhālaṃkṛtaṃ sūryasahasrātirekaprabhaṃ jaṅgamam iva ratnaparvataṃ samantato bhadrakam | [AvŚat, 7 6.2]
sahadarśanāc ca ārāmikeṇa tat padmaṃ bhagavati kṣiptam | [AvŚat, 7 6.3]
tataḥ kṣiptamātraṃ śakaṭacakramāṇaṃ bhūtvā upari bhagavataḥ sthitam | [AvŚat, 7 6.4]
atha sa ārāmikas tat pratihāryaṃ dṛṣṭvā mūlanikṛtta iva drumo bhagavataḥ pādayor nipatya kṛtakarapuṭaś cetanāṃ puṣṇāti praṇidhiṃ ca kartum ārabdhaḥ anenāhaṃ kuśalamūlena cittotpādena deyadharmaparityāgena ca andhe loke anāyake apariṇāyake buddho bhūyāsam atīrṇānāṃ sattvānāṃ tārayitāmuktānāṃ mocayitā anāśvastānām āśvāsayitā aparinirvṛtānāṃ parinirvāpayiteti | [AvŚat, 7 7.1]
atha bhagavāṃs tasyārāmikasya hetuparaṃparāṃ karmaparaṃparāṃ ca jñātvā smitaṃ prāvirakārṣīt | [AvŚat, 7 8.1]
dharmatā khalu yasmin samaye buddhā bhagavantaḥ smitaṃ prāviṣkurvanti tasmin samaye nīlapītalohitāvadātā arciṣo mukhān niścārya kāścid adhastād gacchanti kāścid upariṣṭād gacchanti | [AvŚat, 7 8.2]
yā adhastād gacchanti tāḥ saṃjīvaṃ kālasūtraṃ saṃghātaṃ rauravaṃ mahārauravaṃ tapanaṃ pratāpanam avīcim arbudaṃ nirarbudaṃ aṭaṭaṃ hahavaṃ huhuvam utpalaṃ padmaṃ mahāpadmaṃ narakān gatvā ye uṣṇanarakās teṣu śītībhūtā nipatanti ye śītanarakās teṣūṣṇībhūtā nipatanti | [AvŚat, 7 8.3]
tena teṣāṃ sattvānāṃ kāraṇāviśeṣāḥ pratiprasrabhyante | [AvŚat, 7 8.4]
teṣām evaṃ bhavati kiṃ nu vayaṃ bhavanta itaś cyutāḥ āhosvid anyatropapannā iti | [AvŚat, 7 8.5]
teṣāṃ prasādasaṃjananārthaṃ bhagavān nirmitaṃ visarjayati | [AvŚat, 7 8.6]
teṣāṃ nirmitaṃ dṛṣṭvaivaṃ bhavati na hy eva vayaṃ bhavanta itaś cyutā nāpy anyatropapannāḥ | [AvŚat, 7 8.7]
api tv ayam apūrvadarśanaḥ sattvaḥ asyānubhāvenāsmākaṃ kāraṇāviśeṣāḥ pratiprasrabdhā iti | [AvŚat, 7 8.8]
te nirmite cittam abhiprasādya tan narakavedanīyaṃ karma kṣapayitvā devamanuṣyeṣu pratisandhiṃ gṛhṇanti yatra satyānāṃ bhājanabhūtā bhavanti | [AvŚat, 7 8.9]
yā upariṣṭād gacchanti tāś cāturmahārājikāṃs trayastriṃśān yāmāṃs tuṣitān nirmāṇaratīn paranirmitavaśavartino brahmakāyikān brahmapurohitān mahābrahmaṇaḥ parīttābhān apramāṇābhān ābhāsvarān parīttaśubhān apramāṇaśubhāñ śubhakṛtsnān anabhrakān puṇyaprasavān bṛhatphalān abṛhān atapān sudṛśān sudarśanān akaniṣṭhān devān gatvā anityaṃ duḥkhaṃ śūnyam anātmety udghoṣayanti gāthādvayaṃ ca bhāṣante | [AvŚat, 7 8.10]
ārabhadhvaṃ niṣkrāmata yujyadhvaṃ buddhaśāsane | [AvŚat, 7 8.11]
dhunīta mṛtyunaḥ sainyaṃ naḍāgāram iva kuñjaraḥ | [AvŚat, 7 8.12]
yo hy asmin dharmavinaye apramattaś cariṣyati | [AvŚat, 7 9.1]
prahāya jātisaṃsāraṃ duḥkhasyāntaṃ kariṣyati | [AvŚat, 7 9.2]
atha tā arciṣas trisāhasramahāsāhasraṃ lokadhātum anvāhiṇḍya bhagavantam eva pṛṣṭhataḥ pṛṣṭhataḥ samanugacchanti | [AvŚat, 7 10.1]
tad yadi bhagavān atītaṃ karma vyākartukāmo bhavati bhagavataḥ pṛṣṭhato 'ntardhīyante | [AvŚat, 7 10.2]
anāgataṃ vyākartukāmo bhavati purastād antardhīyante | [AvŚat, 7 10.3]
narakopapattiṃ vyākartukāmo bhavati pādatale 'ntardhīyante | [AvŚat, 7 10.4]
tiryagupapattiṃ vyākartukāmo bhavati pārṣṇyām antardhīyante | [AvŚat, 7 10.5]
pretopapattiṃ vyākartukāmo bhavati pādāṅguṣṭhe 'ntardhīyante | [AvŚat, 7 10.6]
manuṣyopapattiṃ vyākartukāmo bhavati jānunor antardhīyante | [AvŚat, 7 10.7]
balacakravartirājyaṃ vyākartukāmo bhavati vāme karatale 'ntardhīyante | [AvŚat, 7 10.8]
cakravartirājyaṃ vyākartukāmo bhavati dakṣiṇe karatale 'ntardhīyante | [AvŚat, 7 10.9]
devopapattiṃ vyākartukāmo bhavati nābhyām antardhīyante | [AvŚat, 7 10.10]
śrāvakabodhiṃ vyākartukāmo bhavati āsye 'ntardhīyante | [AvŚat, 7 10.11]
pratyekabodhiṃ vyākartukāmo bhavati ūrṇāyām antardhīyante | [AvŚat, 7 10.12]
anuttarāṃ samyaksaṃbodhiṃ vyākartukāmo bhavati uṣṇīṣe antardhīyante | [AvŚat, 7 10.13]
atha tā arciṣo bhagavantaṃ triḥ pradakṣiṇīkṛtya bhagavata uṣṇīṣe 'ntarhitāḥ | [AvŚat, 7 11.1]
athāyuṣmān ānandaḥ kṛtakarapuṭo bhagavantaṃ papraccha | [AvŚat, 7 11.2]
nānāvidho raṅgasahasracitro vaktrāntarān niṣkasitaḥ kalāpaḥ | [AvŚat, 7 11.3]
avabhāsitā yena diśaḥ samantād divākareṇodayatā yathaiva | [AvŚat, 7 11.4]
gāthāś ca bhāṣate | [AvŚat, 7 12.1]
vigatodbhavā dainyamadaprahīṇā buddhā jagaty uttamahetubhūtāḥ | [AvŚat, 7 12.2]
nākāraṇaṃ śaṅkhamṛṇālagauraṃ smitam upadarśayanti jinā jitārayaḥ | [AvŚat, 7 12.3]
tatkālaṃ svayam adhigamya vīra buddhyā śrotṝṇāṃ śramaṇa jinendra kāṅkṣitānām | [AvŚat, 7 13.1]
dhīrābhir munivṛṣa vāgbhir uttamābhir utpannaṃ vyapanaya saṃśayaṃ śubhābhiḥ | [AvŚat, 7 13.2]
nākasmāl lavaṇajalādrirājadhairyāḥ saṃbuddhāḥ smitam upadarśayanti nāthāḥ | [AvŚat, 7 14.1]
yasyārthe smitam upadarśayanti dhīrāḥ taṃ śrotuṃ samabhilaṣanti te janaughāḥ | [AvŚat, 7 14.2]
bhagavān āha evam etad ānanda evam etat | [AvŚat, 7 15.1]
nāhetvapratyayam ānanda tathāgatā arhantaḥ samyaksaṃbuddhāḥ smitaṃ prāviṣkurvanti | [AvŚat, 7 15.2]
paśyasy ānanda anenārāmikeṇa prasādajātena mamaivaṃvidhāṃ pūjām kṛtām | [AvŚat, 7 15.3]
evaṃ bhadanta | [AvŚat, 7 15.4]
eṣa ārāmiko 'nena kuśalamūlena cittotpādena deyadharmaparityāgena ca trikalpāsaṃkhyeyasamudānītāṃ bodhiṃ samudānīya mahākaruṇāparibhāvitāḥ ṣaṭ pāramitāḥ paripūrya padmottamo nāma samyaksaṃbuddho bhaviṣyati daśabhir balaiś caturbhir vaiśāradyais tribhir āveṇikaiḥ smṛtyupasthānair mahākaruṇayā ca | [AvŚat, 7 15.5]
ayam asya deyadharmo yo mamāntike cittaprasāda iti | [AvŚat, 7 15.6]
idam avocad bhagavān | [AvŚat, 7 16.1]
āttamanasas te bhikṣavo bhagavato bhāṣitam abhyanandan | [AvŚat, 7 16.2]
{AvŚat, 8}
buddho bhagavān satkṛto gurukṛto mānitaḥ pūjito rājabhī rājamātrair dhanibhiḥ pauraiḥ śreṣṭhibhiḥ sārthavāhair devair nāgair yakṣair asurair garuḍaiḥ kinnarair mahoragair iti devanāgayakṣāsuragaruḍakinnaramahoragābhyarcito buddho bhagavān jñāto mahāpuṇyo lābhī cīvarapiṇḍapātaśayanāsanaglānapratyayabhaiṣajyapariṣkārāṇāṃ saśrāvakasaṃghaḥ śrāvastyāṃ viharati jetavane 'nāthapiṇḍadasyārāme | [AvŚat, 8 1.1]
tena khalu samayenottarapañcālarājo dakṣiṇapañcālarājena saha prativiruddho babhūva | [AvŚat, 8 2.1]
atha rājā prasenajit kauśalyo yena bhagavāṃs tenopasaṃkrāntaḥ | [AvŚat, 8 2.2]
upasaṃkramya bhagavataḥ pādau śirasā vanditvā ekānte niṣaṇṇaḥ | [AvŚat, 8 2.3]
ekānte niṣaṇṇo rājā prasenajit kauśalyo bhagavantam idam avocat bhagavān nāma bhadanta anuttaro dharmarājo vyasanagatānāṃ sattvānāṃ paritrātā anyonyavairiṇāṃ vairapraśamayitā | [AvŚat, 8 2.4]
ayaṃ cottarapañcālo rājā dakṣiṇapañcālarājena saha prativiruddhaḥ | [AvŚat, 8 2.5]
tau parasparam eva mahājanavipraghātaṃ kurutaḥ | [AvŚat, 8 2.6]
tayor bhagavān dīrgharātrānugatasya vairasyopaśamaṃ kuryād anukampām upādāyeti | [AvŚat, 8 2.7]
adhivāsayati bhagavān rājñaḥ prasenajitaḥ kauśalyasya tūṣṇībhāvena | [AvŚat, 8 2.8]
atha rājā prasenajit kauśalyo bhagavatas tūṣṇībhāvenādhivāsanāṃ viditvā bhagavataḥ pādau śirasā vanditvotthāyāsanāt prakrāntaḥ | [AvŚat, 8 2.9]
atha bhagavāṃs tasyā eva rātrer atyayāt pūrvāhṇe nivāsya pātracīvaram ādāya yena vārāṇasī kāśīnāṃ nagaraṃ tena cārikāṃ prakrāntaḥ | [AvŚat, 8 3.1]
anupūrveṇa cārikāṃ caran vārāṇasīm anuprāpto vārāṇasyāṃ viharati ṛṣipatane mṛgadāve | [AvŚat, 8 3.2]
yāvat tayor viditaṃ bhagavān asmadvijitam anuprāpta iti | [AvŚat, 8 3.3]
yāvad bhagavatā ṛddhibalena caturaṅgabalakāyaṃ nirmāyottarapañcālarājas trāsitaḥ | [AvŚat, 8 3.4]
sa bhīta ekaratham abhiruhya bhagavatsakāśam upasaṃkrāntaḥ | [AvŚat, 8 3.5]
tasya bhagavatā vairapraśamāya dharmo deśitaḥ | [AvŚat, 8 3.6]
sa taṃ dharmaṃ śrutvā bhagavatsakāśe pravrajitaḥ | [AvŚat, 8 3.7]
tena yujyamānena ghaṭamānena vyāyacchamānena sarvakleśaprahāṇād arhattvaṃ sākṣātkṛtam | [AvŚat, 8 3.8]
dakṣiṇapañcālarājenāpi bhagavān saśrāvakasaṃghas traimāsyaṃ śatarasenāhāreṇopanimantritaḥ śatasahasreṇa ca vastreṇācchāditaḥ | [AvŚat, 8 4.1]
praṇidhānaṃ kṛtam anenāhaṃ kuśalamūlena cittotpādena deyadharmaparityāgena ca andhe loke anāyake apariṇāyake buddho bhūyāsam atīrṇānāṃ sattvānāṃ tārayitāmuktānāṃ mocayitā anāśvastānām āśvāsayitā aparinirvṛtānāṃ parinirvāpayiteti | [AvŚat, 8 4.2]
atha bhagavān dakṣiṇapañcālarājasya hetuparaṃparāṃ karmaparaṃparāṃ ca jñātvā smitaṃ prāvirakārṣīt | [AvŚat, 8 5.1]
dharmatā khalu yasmin samaye buddhā bhagavantaḥ smitaṃ prāviṣkurvanti tasmin samaye nīlapītalohitāvadātā arciṣo mukhān niścārya kāścid adhastād gacchanti kāścid upariṣṭād gacchanti | [AvŚat, 8 5.2]
yā adhastād gacchanti tāḥ saṃjīvaṃ kālasūtraṃ saṃghātaṃ rauravaṃ mahārauravaṃ tapanaṃ pratāpanam avīcim arbudaṃ nirarbudaṃ aṭaṭaṃ hahavaṃ huhuvam utpalaṃ padmaṃ mahāpadmaṃ narakān gatvā ye uṣṇanarakās teṣu śītībhūtā nipatanti ye śītanarakās teṣūṣṇībhūtā nipatanti | [AvŚat, 8 5.3]
tena teṣāṃ sattvānāṃ kāraṇāviśeṣāḥ pratiprasrabhyante | [AvŚat, 8 5.4]
teṣām evaṃ bhavati kiṃ nu vayaṃ bhavanta itaś cyutāḥ āhosvid anyatropapannā iti | [AvŚat, 8 5.5]
teṣāṃ prasādasaṃjananārthaṃ bhagavān nirmitaṃ visarjayati | [AvŚat, 8 5.6]
teṣāṃ nirmitaṃ dṛṣṭvā ca evaṃ bhavati na hy eva vayaṃ bhavanta itaś cyutā nāpy anyatropapannāḥ | [AvŚat, 8 5.7]
api tv ayam apūrvadarśanaḥ sattvaḥ asyānubhāvenāsmākaṃ kāraṇāviśeṣāḥ pratiprasrabdhā iti | [AvŚat, 8 5.8]
te nirmite cittam abhiprasādya tan narakavedanīyaṃ karma kṣapayitvā devamanuṣyeṣu pratisandhiṃ gṛhṇanti yatra satyānāṃ bhājanabhūtā bhavanti | [AvŚat, 8 5.9]
yā upariṣṭād gacchanti tāś cāturmahārājikāṃs trayastriṃśān yāmāṃs tuṣitān nirmāṇaratīn paranirmitavaśavartino brahmakāyikān brahmapurohitān mahābrahmaṇaḥ parīttābhān apramāṇābhān ābhāsvarān parīttaśubhān apramāṇaśubhāñ śubhakṛtsnān anabhrakān puṇyaprasavān bṛhatphalān abṛhān atapān sudṛśān sudarśanān akaniṣṭhān devān gatvā anityaṃ duḥkhaṃ śūnyam anātmety udghoṣayanti gāthādvayaṃ ca bhāṣante | [AvŚat, 8 5.10]
ārabhadhvaṃ niṣkrāmata yujyadhvaṃ buddhaśāsane | [AvŚat, 8 5.11]
dhunīta mṛtyunaḥ sainyaṃ naḍāgāram iva kuñjaraḥ | [AvŚat, 8 5.12]
yo hy asmin dharmavinaye apramattaś cariṣyati | [AvŚat, 8 6.1]
prahāya jātisaṃsāraṃ duḥkhasyāntaṃ kariṣyati | [AvŚat, 8 6.2]
atha tā arciṣas trisāhasramahāsāhasraṃ lokadhātum anvāhiṇḍya bhagavantam eva pṛṣṭhataḥ pṛṣṭhataḥ samanugacchanti | [AvŚat, 8 7.1]
tad yadi bhagavān atītaṃ karma vyākartukāmo bhavati bhagavataḥ pṛṣṭhato 'ntardhīyante | [AvŚat, 8 7.2]
anāgataṃ vyākartukāmo bhavati purastād antardhīyante | [AvŚat, 8 7.3]
narakopapattiṃ vyākartukāmo bhavati pādatale 'ntardhīyante | [AvŚat, 8 7.4]
tiryagupapattiṃ vyākartukāmo bhavati pārṣṇyām antardhīyante | [AvŚat, 8 7.5]
pretopapattiṃ vyākartukāmo bhavati pādāṅguṣṭhe 'ntardhīyante | [AvŚat, 8 7.6]
manuṣyopapattiṃ vyākartukāmo bhavati jānunor antardhīyante | [AvŚat, 8 7.7]
balacakravartirājyaṃ vyākartukāmo bhavati vāme karatale 'ntardhīyante | [AvŚat, 8 7.8]
cakravartirājyaṃ vyākartukāmo bhavati dakṣiṇe karatale 'ntardhīyante | [AvŚat, 8 7.9]
devopapattiṃ vyākartukāmo bhavati nābhyām antardhīyante | [AvŚat, 8 7.10]
śrāvakabodhiṃ vyākartukāmo bhavati āsye 'ntardhīyante | [AvŚat, 8 7.11]
pratyekabodhiṃ vyākartukāmo bhavati ūrṇāyām antardhīyante | [AvŚat, 8 7.12]
anuttarāṃ samyaksaṃbodhiṃ vyākartukāmo bhavati uṣṇīṣe antardhīyante | [AvŚat, 8 7.13]
atha tā arciṣo bhagavantaṃ triḥ pradakṣiṇīkṛtya bhagavata uṣṇīṣe 'ntarhitāḥ | [AvŚat, 8 8.1]
athāyuṣmān ānandaḥ kṛtakarapuṭo bhagavantaṃ papraccha | [AvŚat, 8 8.2]
nānāvidho raṅgasahasracitro vaktrāntarān niṣkasitaḥ kalāpaḥ | [AvŚat, 8 8.3]
avabhāsitā yena diśaḥ samantād divākareṇodayatā yathaiva | [AvŚat, 8 8.4]
gāthāś ca bhāṣate | [AvŚat, 8 9.1]
vigatodbhavā dainyamadaprahīṇā buddhā jagaty uttamahetubhūtāḥ | [AvŚat, 8 9.2]
nākāraṇaṃ śaṅkhamṛṇālagauraṃ smitam upadarśayanti jinā jitārayaḥ | [AvŚat, 8 9.3]
tatkālaṃ svayam adhigamya vīra buddhyā śrotṝṇāṃ śramaṇa jinendra kāṅkṣitānām | [AvŚat, 8 10.1]
dhīrābhir munivṛṣa vāgbhir uttamābhirutpannaṃ vyapanaya saṃśayaṃ śubhābhiḥ | [AvŚat, 8 10.2]
nākasmāl lavaṇajalādrirājadhairyāḥ saṃbuddhāḥ smitam upadarśayanti nāthāḥ | [AvŚat, 8 11.1]
yasyārthe smitam upadarśayanti dhīrāḥ taṃ śrotuṃ samabhilaṣanti te janaughāḥ | [AvŚat, 8 11.2]
bhagavān āha evam etad ānanda evam etat | [AvŚat, 8 12.1]
nāhetvapratyayam ānanda tathāgatā arhantaḥ samyaksaṃbuddhāḥ smitaṃ prāviṣkurvanti | [AvŚat, 8 12.2]
paśyasy ānanda dakṣiṇapañcālarājena mamaivaṃvidhaṃ satkāraṃ kṛtam | [AvŚat, 8 12.3]
evaṃ bhadanta | [AvŚat, 8 12.4]
eṣa ānanda pañcālarājo 'nena kuśalamūlena cittotpādena deyadharmaparityāgena ca trikalpāsaṃkhyeyasamudānītāṃ bodhiṃ samudānīya mahākaruṇāparibhāvitāḥ ṣaṭ pāramitāḥ paripūrya vijayo nāma samyaksaṃbuddho bhaviṣyati daśabhir balaiś caturbhir vaiśāradyais tribhir āveṇikaiḥ smṛtyupasthānair mahākaruṇayā ca | [AvŚat, 8 12.5]
ayam asya deyadharmo yo mamāntike cittaprasādaḥ | [AvŚat, 8 12.6]
idam avocad bhagavān | [AvŚat, 8 13.1]
āttamanasas te bhikṣavo bhagavato bhāṣitam abhyanandan | [AvŚat, 8 13.2]
{AvŚat, 9}
buddho bhagavān satkṛto gurukṛto mānitaḥ pūjito rājabhī rājamātrair dhanibhiḥ pauraiḥ śreṣṭhibhiḥ sārthavāhair devair nāgair yakṣair asurair garuḍaiḥ kinnarair mahoragair iti devanāgayakṣāsuragaruḍakinnaramahoragābhyarcito buddho bhagavān jñāto mahāpuṇyo lābhī cīvarapiṇḍapātaśayanāsanaglānapratyayabhaiṣajyapariṣkārāṇāṃ saśrāvakasaṃghaḥ śrāvastyāṃ viharati jetavane 'nāthapiṇḍadasyārāme | [AvŚat, 9 1.1]
tena khalu samayena śrāvastyāṃ dvau śreṣṭhinau | [AvŚat, 9 2.1]
tāv anyonyaṃ prativiruddhau babhūvatuḥ | [AvŚat, 9 2.2]
tābhyām ekaḥ pūraṇe 'bhiprasannaḥ dvitīyo buddhe bhagavati | [AvŚat, 9 2.3]
tatas tayoḥ parasparaṃ kathāsāṃkathyaviniścaye vartamāne pūraṇopāsaka āha buddhāt pūraṇo viśiṣṭatara iti | [AvŚat, 9 2.4]
buddhopāsaka āha bhagavān samyaksaṃbuddho viśiṣṭatara iti | [AvŚat, 9 2.5]
tatas tābhyāṃ sarvasvāpaharaṇe bandhanikṣepaḥ kṛtaḥ | [AvŚat, 9 2.6]
yāvad rājñaḥ prasenajitaḥ śrutam | [AvŚat, 9 3.1]
tenāmātyānām ājñā dattā tayor mīmāṃsā kartavyeti | [AvŚat, 9 3.2]
tatas tair amātyaiḥ sarvavijite ghaṇṭāvaghoṣaṇaṃ kāritam saptame divase buddhatīrthikopāsakayor mīmāṃsā bhaviṣyati ye cādbhutāni draṣṭukāmās te āgacchantv iti | [AvŚat, 9 3.3]
tataḥ saptame divase vistīrṇāvakāśe pṛthivīpradeśe 'nekeṣu prāṇiśatasahasreṣu saṃnipatiteṣu gaganatale cānekeṣu devatāsahasreṣu saṃnipatiteṣu gomayamaṇḍalake kﾱpte sarvagandhamālyeṣūpahṛteṣu pūrvataraṃ tīrthikopāsakena satyopayācanaṃ kṛtam yena satyena pūraṇaprabhṛtayaḥ ṣaṭ śāstāro loke śreṣṭhāḥ anena satyenemāni puṣpāṇi ayaṃ ca dhūpaḥ idaṃ ca pānīyaṃ tān upagacchantv iti | [AvŚat, 9 3.4]
tato mahājanakāyena kilakilāprakṣveḍoccair nādo muktaḥ yam abhivīkṣya tīrthyopāsakas tuṣṇībhūto maṅkubhūtaḥ srastaskandho 'dhomukho niṣpratibhānaḥ pradhyānaparamaḥ kare kapolaṃ dattvā cintāparo vyavasthitaḥ | [AvŚat, 9 4.1]
tato bhagavacchrāvakeṇa harṣotkaṇṭhajātena prasādavikasitābhyāṃ nayanābhyām ekāṃsam uttarāsaṅgaṃ kṛtvā dakṣiṇajānumaṇḍalaṃ pṛthivyāṃ pratiṣṭhāpya satyopayācanaṃ kṛtam yena satyena bhagavān sarvasattvānām agryaḥ anena satyenemāni puṣpāṇi dhūpa udakaṃ bhagavantam upagacchantv iti | [AvŚat, 9 5.1]
evaṃ pravyāhṛtamātre tāni puṣpāṇi haṃsapaṅktir ivākāśe jetavanābhimukhaṃ samprasthitāni dhūpo 'bhrakūṭavat udakaṃ vaiḍūryaśalākavat | [AvŚat, 9 5.2]
atha sa mahājanakāyas tat prātihāryaṃ dṛṣṭvā kilakilāprakṣveḍoccaiḥśabdaṃ kurvaṃs teṣāṃ samprasthitānāṃ pṛṣṭhataḥ pṛṣṭhataḥ samanubaddhaḥ | [AvŚat, 9 5.3]
tatas tāni puṣpāṇi bhagavata upari sthitāni dhūpa udakaṃ cāgrataḥ | [AvŚat, 9 6.1]
tataḥ sa mahājanakāyo labdhaprasādo bhagavataḥ pādābhivandanaṃ kṛtvā purastān niṣaṇṇo dharmaśravaṇāya | [AvŚat, 9 6.2]
teṣāṃ bhagavān idaṃ sūtraṃ bhāṣate sma | [AvŚat, 9 6.3]
tisra imā brāhmaṇagṛhapatayo 'graprajñaptayaḥ | [AvŚat, 9 6.4]
katamās tisraḥ buddhe agraprajñaptiḥ dharme saṃghe agraprajñaptiḥ | [AvŚat, 9 6.5]
buddhe agraprajñaptiḥ katamā ye kecid brāhmaṇagṛhapatayaḥ sattvā apadā vā dvipadā vā bahupadā vā rūpiṇo vā arūpiṇo vā saṃjñino vā asaṃjñino vā naivasaṃjñino nāsaṃjñinaḥ tathāgato 'rhan samyaksaṃbuddhas teṣām agra ākhyātaḥ | [AvŚat, 9 6.6]
ye kecid buddhe 'bhiprasannāḥ agre te 'bhiprasannāḥ | [AvŚat, 9 6.7]
teṣām agre 'bhiprasannānām agra eva vipākaḥ pratikāṅkṣitavyo deveṣu vā devabhūtānāṃ manuṣyeṣu vā manuṣyabhūtānām | [AvŚat, 9 6.8]
iyam ucyate brāhmaṇagṛhapatayo buddhe agraprajñaptiḥ | [AvŚat, 9 6.9]
dharme agraprajñaptiḥ katamā ye kecid dharmāḥ saṃskṛtā vā asaṃskṛtā vā virāgo dharmas teṣām agra ākhyātaḥ | [AvŚat, 9 6.10]
ye kecid dharme 'bhiprasannā agre te 'bhiprasannāḥ | [AvŚat, 9 6.11]
teṣām agre 'bhiprasannānām agra eva vipākaḥ pratikāṅkṣitavyo deveṣu vā devabhūtānāṃ manuṣyeṣu vā manuṣyabhūtānām | [AvŚat, 9 6.12]
iyam ucyate brāhmaṇagṛhapatayo dharme agraprajñaptiḥ | [AvŚat, 9 6.13]
saṃgheṣu agraprajñaptiḥ katamā ye kecit saṃghā vā gaṇā vā pūgā vā pariṣado vā tathāgataśrāvakasaṃghas teṣām agra ākhyātaḥ | [AvŚat, 9 6.14]
ye kecit saṃghe 'bhiprasannāḥ agre te 'bhiprasannāḥ | [AvŚat, 9 6.15]
teṣām agre 'bhiprasannānām agra eva vipākaḥ pratikāṅkṣitavyo deveṣu vā devabhūtānāṃ manuṣyeṣu vā manuṣyabhūtānām | [AvŚat, 9 6.16]
iyam ucyate brāhmaṇagṛhapatayaḥ saṃghe agraprajñaptiḥ | [AvŚat, 9 6.17]
asmin khalu dharmaparyāye bhāṣyamāṇe teṣāṃ brāhmaṇagṛhapatīnāṃ kaiścid buddhadharmasaṃgheṣu prasādaḥ pratilabdhaḥ kaiściccharaṇagamanaśikṣāpadāni gṛhītāni kaiścit pravrajya idam eva pañcagaṇḍakaṃ saṃsāracakraṃ calācalaṃ viditvā sarvasaṃskāragatīḥ śatanapatanavikaraṇavidhvaṃsanadharmatayā parāhatya sarvakleśaprahāṇād arhattvaṃ sākṣātkṛtam | [AvŚat, 9 6.18]
tena ca tīrthyopāsakena tathāgatāntike prasādaḥ pratilabdhaḥ | [AvŚat, 9 6.19]
tato mūlanikṛtta iva drumaḥ bhagavataḥ pādayor nipatya praṇidhānaṃ kartum ārabdhaḥ anenāhaṃ kuśalamūlena cittotpādena deyadharmaparityāgena ca andhe loke anāyake apariṇāyake buddho bhūyāsam atīrṇānāṃ sattvānāṃ tārayitā amuktānāṃ mocayitā anāśvastānām āśvāsayitā aparinirvṛtānāṃ parinirvāpayiteti | [AvŚat, 9 6.20]
atha bhagavāṃs tasya tīrthikopāsakasya hetuparaṃparāṃ karmaparaṃparāṃ ca jñātvā smitaṃ prāvirakārṣīt | [AvŚat, 9 7.1]
dharmatā khalu yasmin samaye buddhā bhagavantaḥ smitaṃ prāviṣkurvanti tasmin samaye nīlapītalohitāvadātā arciṣo mukhān niścārya kāścid adhastād gacchanti kāścid upariṣṭād gacchanti | [AvŚat, 9 7.2]
yā adhastād gacchanti tāḥ saṃjīvaṃ kālasūtraṃ saṃghātaṃ rauravaṃ mahārauravaṃ tapanaṃ pratāpanam avīcim arbudaṃ nirarbudaṃ aṭaṭaṃ hahavaṃ huhuvam utpalaṃ padmaṃ mahāpadmaṃ narakān gatvā ye uṣṇanarakāsteṣu śītībhūtā nipatanti ye śītanarakās teṣūṣṇībhūtā nipatanti | [AvŚat, 9 7.3]
tena teṣāṃ sattvānāṃ kāraṇāviśeṣāḥ pratiprasrabhyante | [AvŚat, 9 7.4]
teṣām evaṃ bhavati kiṃ nu vayaṃ bhavanta itaś cyutāḥ āhosvid anyatropapannā iti | [AvŚat, 9 7.5]
teṣāṃ prasādasaṃjananārthaṃ bhagavān nirmitaṃ visarjayati | [AvŚat, 9 7.6]
teṣāṃ nirmitaṃ dṛṣṭvaivaṃ bhavati na hy eva vayaṃ bhavanta itaś cyutā nāpy anyatropapannāḥ | [AvŚat, 9 7.7]
api tv ayam apūrvadarśanaḥ sattvaḥ asyānubhāvenāsmākaṃ kāraṇāviśeṣāḥ pratiprasrabdhā iti | [AvŚat, 9 7.8]
te nirmite cittam abhiprasādya tan narakavedanīyaṃ karma kṣapayitvā devamanuṣyeṣu pratisandhiṃ gṛhṇanti yatra satyānāṃ bhājanabhūtā bhavanti | [AvŚat, 9 7.9]
yā upariṣṭād gacchanti tāś cāturmahārājikāṃs trayastriṃśān yāmāṃs tuṣitān nirmāṇaratīn paranirmitavaśavartino brahmakāyikān brahmapurohitān mahābrahmaṇaḥ parīttābhān apramāṇābhān ābhāsvarān parīttaśubhān apramāṇaśubhāñ śubhakṛtsnān anabhrakān puṇyaprasavān bṛhatphalān abṛhān atapān sudṛśān sudarśanān akaniṣṭhān devān gatvā anityaṃ duḥkhaṃ śūnyam anātmety udghoṣayanti gāthādvayaṃ ca bhāṣante | [AvŚat, 9 7.10]
ārabhadhvaṃ niṣkrāmata yujyadhvaṃ buddhaśāsane | [AvŚat, 9 7.11]
dhunīta mṛtyunaḥ sainyaṃ naḍāgāram iva kuñjaraḥ | [AvŚat, 9 7.12]
yo hy asmin dharmavinaye apramattaś cariṣyati | [AvŚat, 9 8.1]
prahāya jātisaṃsāraṃ duḥkhasyāntaṃ kariṣyati | [AvŚat, 9 8.2]
atha tā arciṣas trisāhasramahāsāhasraṃ lokadhātum anvāhiṇḍya bhagavantam eva pṛṣṭhataḥ pṛṣṭhataḥ samanugacchanti | [AvŚat, 9 9.1]
tad yadi bhagavān atītaṃ karma vyākartukāmo bhavati bhagavataḥ pṛṣṭhato 'ntardhīyante | [AvŚat, 9 9.2]
anāgataṃ vyākartukāmo bhavati purastād antardhīyante | [AvŚat, 9 9.3]
narakopapattiṃ vyākartukāmo bhavati pādatale 'ntardhīyante | [AvŚat, 9 9.4]
tiryagupapattiṃ vyākartukāmo bhavati pārṣṇyām antardhīyante | [AvŚat, 9 9.5]
pretopapattiṃ vyākartukāmo bhavati pādāṅguṣṭhe 'ntardhīyante | [AvŚat, 9 9.6]
manuṣyopapattiṃ vyākartukāmo bhavati jānunor antardhīyante | [AvŚat, 9 9.7]
balacakravartirājyaṃ vyākartukāmo bhavati vāme karatale 'ntardhīyante | [AvŚat, 9 9.8]
cakravartirājyaṃ vyākartukāmo bhavati dakṣiṇe karatale 'ntardhīyante | [AvŚat, 9 9.9]
devopapattiṃ vyākartukāmo bhavati nābhyām antardhīyante | [AvŚat, 9 9.10]
śrāvakabodhiṃ vyākartukāmo bhavati āsye 'ntardhīyante | [AvŚat, 9 9.11]
pratyekabodhiṃ vyākartukāmo bhavati ūrṇāyām antardhīyante | [AvŚat, 9 9.12]
anuttarāṃ samyaksaṃbodhiṃ vyākartukāmo bhavati uṣṇīṣe antardhīyante | [AvŚat, 9 9.13]
atha tā arciṣo bhagavantaṃ triḥ pradakṣiṇīkṛtya bhagavata uṣṇīṣe 'ntarhitāḥ | [AvŚat, 9 10.1]
athāyuṣmān ānandaḥ kṛtakarapuṭo bhagavantaṃ papraccha | [AvŚat, 9 10.2]
nānāvidho raṅgasahasracitro vaktrāntarān niṣkasitaḥ kalāpaḥ | [AvŚat, 9 10.3]
avabhāsitā yena diśaḥ samantād divākareṇodayatā yathaiva | [AvŚat, 9 10.4]
gāthāś ca bhāṣate | [AvŚat, 9 11.1]
vigatodbhavā dainyamadaprahīṇā buddhā jagaty uttamahetubhūtāḥ | [AvŚat, 9 11.2]
nākāraṇaṃ śaṅkhamṛṇālagauraṃ smitam upadarśayanti jinā jitārayaḥ | [AvŚat, 9 11.3]
tatkālaṃ svayam adhigamya vīra buddhyā śrotṝṇāṃ śramaṇa jinendra kāṅkṣitānām | [AvŚat, 9 12.1]
dhīrābhir munivṛṣa vāgbhir uttamābhir utpannaṃ vyapanaya saṃśayaṃ śubhābhiḥ | [AvŚat, 9 12.2]
nākasmāl lavaṇajalādrirājadhairyāḥ saṃbuddhāḥ smitam upadarśayanti nāthāḥ | [AvŚat, 9 13.1]
yasyārthe smitam upadarśayanti dhīrāḥ taṃ śrotuṃ samabhilaṣanti te janaughāḥ | [AvŚat, 9 13.2]
bhagavān āha evam etad ānanda evam etat | [AvŚat, 9 14.1]
nāhetvapratyayam ānanda tathāgatā arhantaḥ samyaksaṃbuddhāḥ smitaṃ prāviṣkurvanti | [AvŚat, 9 14.2]
paśyasy ānanda anena tīrthikopāsakena mamaivaṃvidhaṃ satkāraṃ kṛtam | [AvŚat, 9 14.3]
evaṃ bhadanta | [AvŚat, 9 14.4]
eṣa ānanda tīrthopāsako 'nena kuśalamūlena cittotpādena deyadharmaparityāgena ca trikalpāsaṃkhyeyasamudānītāṃ bodhiṃ samudānīya mahākaruṇāparibhāvitāḥ ṣaṭ pāramitāḥ paripūrya acalo nāma samyaksaṃbuddho bhaviṣyati daśabhir balaiś caturbhir vaiśāradyais tribhir āveṇikaiḥ smṛtyupasthānair mahākaruṇayā ca | [AvŚat, 9 14.5]
ayam asya deyadharmo yo mamāntike cittaprasāda iti | [AvŚat, 9 14.6]
idam avocad bhagavān | [AvŚat, 9 15.1]
āttamanasas te bhikṣavo bhagavato bhāṣitam abhyanandan | [AvŚat, 9 15.2]
{AvŚat, 10}
buddho bhagavān satkṛto gurukṛto mānitaḥ pūjito rājabhī rājamātrair dhanibhiḥ pauraiḥ śreṣṭhibhiḥ sārthavāhair devair nāgair yakṣair asurair garuḍaiḥ kinnarair mahoragair iti devanāgayakṣāsuragaruḍakinnaramahoragābhyarcito buddho bhagavān jñāto mahāpuṇyo lābhī cīvarapiṇḍapātaśayanāsanaglānapratyayabhaiṣajyapariṣkārāṇāṃ saśrāvakasaṃghaḥ śrāvastyāṃ viharati jetavane 'nāthapiṇḍadasyārāme | [AvŚat, 10 1.1]
tena khalu samayena rājā prasenajit kauśalo rājā ca ajātaśatruḥ ubhāv apy etau parasparaṃ viruddhau babhūvatuḥ | [AvŚat, 10 1.2]
atha rājā ajātaśatruś caturaṅgabalakāyaṃ saṃnahya hastikāyam aśvakāyaṃ rathakāyaṃ pattikāyaṃ rājānaṃ prasenajitaṃ kauśalam abhiniryāto yuddhāya | [AvŚat, 10 1.3]
aśrauṣīd rājā prasenajit kauśalaḥ rājā ajātaśatruś caturaṅgabalakāyaṃ saṃnahya hastikāyam aśvakāyaṃ rathakāyaṃ pattikāyaṃ ca abhiniryāto yuddhāyeti | [AvŚat, 10 2.1]
śrutvā ca caturaṅgabalakāyaṃ saṃnahya hastikāyam aśvakāyaṃ rathakāyaṃ pattikāyaṃ rājānam ajātaśatruṃ pratyabhiniryāto yuddhāya | [AvŚat, 10 2.2]
atha rājñā ajātaśatruṇā rājñaḥ prasenajitaḥ kauśalasya sarvo hastikāyaḥ paryastaḥ aśvakāyo rathakāyaḥ pattikāyaḥ paryastaḥ | [AvŚat, 10 2.3]
rājā prasenajit kauśalo jito bhīto bhagnaḥ parājitaḥ parāpṛṣṭhīkṛta ekarathena śrāvastīṃ praviṣṭaḥ | [AvŚat, 10 2.4]
evaṃ yāvat trir api | [AvŚat, 10 2.5]
atha rājā prasenajit kauśalaḥ śokāgāraṃ praviśya kare kapolaṃ dattvā cintāparo vyavasthitaḥ | [AvŚat, 10 3.1]
tatra ca śrāvastyām anyatamaḥ śreṣṭhī āḍhyo mahādhano mahābhogo vistīrṇaviśālaparigraho vaiśravaṇadhanasamudito vaiśravaṇadhanapratispardhī | [AvŚat, 10 3.2]
tena śrutaṃ yathā rājā prasenajit kauśalo jito bhagnaḥ parāpṛṣṭhīkṛtaḥ ekaratheneha praviṣṭa iti | [AvŚat, 10 3.3]
śrutvā ca punar yena rājā prasenajit kauśalas tenopasaṃkrāntaḥ | [AvŚat, 10 3.4]
upasaṃkramya rājānaṃ prasenajitaṃ kauśalaṃ jayenāyuṣā ca vardhayitvā ca kimarthaṃ deva śokaḥ kriyate ahaṃ devasya tāvat suvarṇam anuprayacchāmi yena devaḥ punar api yatheṣṭapracāraṇaṃ kariṣyatīti | [AvŚat, 10 3.5]
tena tasya mahān suvarṇarāśiḥ kṛtaḥ yatropaviṣṭaḥ puruṣa utthitaṃ puruṣaṃ na paśyati utthito vā upaviṣṭam | [AvŚat, 10 3.6]
atha rājñā prasenajitkauśalyena svaviṣaye carapuruṣāḥ samantata utsṛṣṭāḥ śṛṇuta janapravādān iti | [AvŚat, 10 4.1]
yāvaj jetavane dvau mallāv anyonyaṃ saṃjalpaṃ kurutaḥ asti kesarī nāma saṃgrāmaḥ | [AvŚat, 10 4.2]
tatra ye kātarāḥ puruṣās te saṃgrāmaśirasi sthāpyante ye madhyās te madhye ye utkṛṣṭāḥ śūrapuruṣās te pṛṣṭhata iti | [AvŚat, 10 4.3]
tatas te rājñe iti veditavantaḥ | [AvŚat, 10 4.4]
śrutvā ca rājā prasenajit kauśalas tathā caturaṅgabalakāyaṃ saṃnāhya hastikāyam aśvakāyaṃ rathakāyaṃ pattikāyaṃ ca rājānam ajātaśatrum abhiniryāto yuddhāya | [AvŚat, 10 4.5]
tato rājñā prasenajitā kauśalena rājño 'jātaśatror vaidehīputrasya sarvo hastikāyaḥ paryastaḥ aśvakāyo rathakāyaḥ pattikāyaḥ paryastaḥ | [AvŚat, 10 4.6]
rājānam apy ajātaśatruṃ vaidehīputraṃ jitaṃ bhītabhagnaparājitaṃ parāpṛṣṭhīkṛtaṃ jīvagrāhaṃ gṛhītvā ekarathe 'bhiropya yena bhagavāṃs tenopasaṃkrāntaḥ | [AvŚat, 10 4.7]
upasaṃkramya bhagavataḥ pādau śirasā vanditvā ekānte niṣīdati | [AvŚat, 10 4.8]
ekāntaniṣaṇṇo rājā prasenajitkauśalo bhagavantam ity avocat ayaṃ hi bhadanta rājā ajātaśatrur dīrgharātram avairasya me vairī asapatnasya sapatnaḥ | [AvŚat, 10 4.9]
na cecchāmy enaṃ jīvitād vyaparopayitum yasmād vayasyaputro 'yaṃ bhavati | [AvŚat, 10 4.10]
muñcāmy enam iti | [AvŚat, 10 4.11]
muñca mahārājety uktvā bhagavāṃstasyāṃ velāyāṃ gāthāṃ bhāṣate | [AvŚat, 10 4.12]
jayo vairaṃ prasavati duḥkhaṃ śete parājitaḥ | [AvŚat, 10 4.13]
upaśāntaḥ sukhaṃ śete hitvā jayaparājayam | [AvŚat, 10 4.14]
atha rājñaḥ prasenajitaḥ kauśalasyaitad abhavat yan mayā rājyaṃ pratilabdham tad asya śreṣṭhinaḥ prasādāt | [AvŚat, 10 5.1]
yannvaham enaṃ vareṇa pravārayeyam iti | [AvŚat, 10 5.2]
atha rājā prasenajit kauśalas taṃ śreṣṭhinaṃ vareṇa pravārayati | [AvŚat, 10 5.3]
sa kathayati ākāṅkṣāmi varam saptāhaṃ me yathābhirucitaṃ rājyam anuprayacchateti | [AvŚat, 10 5.4]
tato rājñā sarvavijite ghaṇṭāvaghoṣaṇaṃ kāritam dattaṃ me śreṣṭhine saptāham ekaṃ rājyam iti | [AvŚat, 10 5.5]
yāvat tena śreṣṭhinā buddhapramukho bhikṣusaṃghaḥ saptāhaṃ bhaktenopanimantritaḥ rājā ca prasenajit saparivāraḥ | [AvŚat, 10 5.6]
yāvantaś ca kāśikośaleṣu janakāyāḥ prativasanti teṣāṃ dūtasaṃpreṣaṇaṃ kṛtam saptāhaṃ yūyaṃ sakalā yatheṣṭacāriṇaḥ sukhasparśaṃ viharata | [AvŚat, 10 5.7]
kiṃcid āgatya buddhaṃ śaraṇaṃ gacchata dharmaṃ ca bhikṣusaṃghaṃ ca | [AvŚat, 10 5.8]
māmakaṃ ca bhojanaṃ bhuñjānās tathāgataṃ paryupāsadhvam iti | [AvŚat, 10 5.9]
tena saptāhaṃ bhagavān saśrāvakasaṃgho mahatā satkāreṇa satkṛtaḥ bahūni ca prāṇiśatasahasrāṇi kuśale niyojitāni | [AvŚat, 10 5.10]
saptāhasyātyayena bhagavataḥ pādayor nipatya cetanāṃ puṣṇāti praṇidhiṃ ca cakāra anenāhaṃ kuśalamūlena cittotpādena deyadharmaparityāgena ca andhe loke anāyake apariṇāyake buddho bhūyāsam atīrṇānāṃ sattvānāṃ tārayitā amuktānāṃ mocayitā anāśvastānām āśvāsayitā aparinirvṛtānāṃ parinirvāpayiteti | [AvŚat, 10 5.11]
atha bhagavāṃs tasya śreṣṭhino hetuparaṃparāṃ karmaparaṃparāṃ ca jñātvā smitaṃ prāvirakārṣīt | [AvŚat, 10 6.1]
dharmatā khalu yasmin samaye buddhā bhagavantaḥ smitaṃ prāviṣkurvanti tasmin samaye nīlapītalohitāvadātā arciṣo mukhān niścārya kāścid adhastād gacchanti kāścid upariṣṭād gacchanti | [AvŚat, 10 6.2]
yā adhastād gacchanti tāḥ saṃjīvaṃ kālasūtraṃ saṃghātaṃ rauravaṃ mahārauravaṃ tapanaṃ pratāpanam avīcim arbudaṃ nirarbudaṃ aṭaṭaṃ hahavaṃ huhuvam utpalaṃ padmaṃ mahāpadmaṃ narakān gatvā ye uṣṇanarakās teṣu śītībhūtā nipatanti ye śītanarakās teṣūṣṇībhūtā nipatanti | [AvŚat, 10 6.3]
tena teṣāṃ sattvānāṃ kāraṇāviśeṣāḥ pratiprasrabhyante | [AvŚat, 10 6.4]
teṣām evaṃ bhavati kiṃ nu vayaṃ bhavanta itaś cyutāḥ āhosvid anyatropapannā iti | [AvŚat, 10 6.5]
teṣāṃ prasādasaṃjananārthaṃ bhagavān nirmitaṃ visarjayati | [AvŚat, 10 6.6]
teṣāṃ nirmitaṃ dṛṣṭvaivaṃ bhavati na hy eva vayaṃ bhavanta itaś cyutā nāpy anyatropapannāḥ | [AvŚat, 10 6.7]
api tv ayam apūrvadarśanaḥ sattvaḥ asyānubhāvenāsmākaṃ kāraṇāviśeṣāḥ pratiprasrabdhā iti | [AvŚat, 10 6.8]
te nirmite cittam abhiprasādya tan narakavedanīyaṃ karma kṣapayitvā devamanuṣyeṣu pratisandhiṃ gṛhṇanti yatra satyānāṃ bhājanabhūtā bhavanti | [AvŚat, 10 6.9]
yā upariṣṭād gacchanti tāś cāturmahārājikāṃs trayastriṃśān yāmāṃs tuṣitān nirmāṇaratīn paranirmitavaśavartino brahmakāyikān brahmapurohitān mahābrahmaṇaḥ parīttābhān apramāṇābhān ābhāsvarān parīttaśubhān apramāṇaśubhāñ śubhakṛtsnān anabhrakān puṇyaprasavān bṛhatphalān abṛhān atapān sudṛśān sudarśanān akaniṣṭhān devān gatvā anityaṃ duḥkhaṃ śūnyam anātmety udghoṣayanti gāthādvayaṃ ca bhāṣante | [AvŚat, 10 6.10]
ārabhadhvaṃ niṣkrāmata yujyadhvaṃ buddhaśāsane | [AvŚat, 10 6.11]
dhunīta mṛtyunaḥ sainyaṃ naḍāgāram iva kuñjaraḥ | [AvŚat, 10 6.12]
yo hy asmin dharmavinaye apramattaś cariṣyati | [AvŚat, 10 7.1]
prahāya jātisaṃsāraṃ duḥkhasyāntaṃ kariṣyati | [AvŚat, 10 7.2]
atha tā arciṣas trisāhasramahāsāhasraṃ lokadhātum anvāhiṇḍya bhagavantam eva pṛṣṭhataḥ pṛṣṭhataḥ samanugacchanti | [AvŚat, 10 8.1]
tad yadi bhagavān atītaṃ karma vyākartukāmo bhavati bhagavataḥ pṛṣṭhato 'ntardhīyante | [AvŚat, 10 8.2]
anāgataṃ karma vyākartukāmo bhavati purastād antardhīyante | [AvŚat, 10 8.3]
narakopapattiṃ vyākartukāmo bhavati pādatale 'ntardhīyante | [AvŚat, 10 8.4]
tiryagupapattiṃ vyākartukāmo bhavati pārṣṇyām antardhīyante | [AvŚat, 10 8.5]
pretopapattiṃ vyākartukāmo bhavati pādāṅguṣṭhe 'ntardhīyante | [AvŚat, 10 8.6]
manuṣyopapattiṃ vyākartukāmo bhavati jānunor antardhīyante | [AvŚat, 10 8.7]
